The Relief Association for the Yellow River Flood Establishes an Office in Shanghai

(Nanjing) The general office of the Yellow River Flood Relief Committee has decided to be established in Shanghai, with five groups under it: general affairs, finance, emergency relief, work relief, and sanitation. It will be established within days, and the position of director will be taken by Zeng Rongpu. (11th Dispatch)

The People of Fengpei County Plan to Block the Dasha River Estuary

The People of Xiaodang County Rise Up in Opposition

Commissioner Yu Has Prohibited the Blocking of the Estuary

(Xuzhou) This time, the Yellow River water came east, entered the old course, and flowed into the Dasha River. Fengpei suffered, while Xiaodang suffered less because of two dams obstructing the water. Now, the people of Fengpei plan to block the Dasha River estuary and simultaneously dredge the two dams. The people of Xiaodang believe that diverting the water harms them and have risen up in opposition, separately petitioning the provincial government, the Xuzhou Garrison Headquarters, and the Commissioner's Office to stop it. Commissioner Yu Nianci has telegraphed the county magistrates of Fengpei and Xiaodang to prohibit the blocking of the Shayang River estuary and report to the provincial government for approval. Currently, the people of the four counties are gathering armed forces to prepare for a dispute over blocking the estuary. Yu has dispatched personnel to Dangshan to investigate and strictly prohibit disputes, and is awaiting further solutions. (11th Dispatch)

(Xuzhou) In the middle of last month, the Yellow River breached its banks in eastern Henan, and the water entered the old course, reaching the Gaozhai and Panlongji dams in the eastern part of Dangshan County. Due to silting downstream, it turned northeast and flowed through the Dasha River in Fengpei into the Zhaowei and Lianghu Lakes. Fortunately, Xuzhou was not affected. Now that the Yellow River water has receded, the party and government organs of Fengpei County are urgently planning to block the Dasha River channel east of Gaozhai and intend to dredge the old Yellow River channel and dikes south of the two dams, allowing the Yellow River water to flow straight down and east through the old course. Recently, the two counties have sent personnel to survey and estimate the work in the area of the two dams and have also investigated and mobilized police and militia to garrison south of the two dams, in order to implement the blocking of the Shayang River and the excavation of the old course. The entire population of Xiaodang County, believing that they are located downstream of the old course, is extremely angry. They have also gathered people, sharpened knives, and polished guns, waiting for a fight. Local organs and legal entities have jointly telegraphed Governor Gu of Jiangsu Province, Commander Zeng of Xuzhou, and Commissioner She to request a strict prohibition, stating that they have investigated and found that the north bank of the Yellow River in Dangshan County, at Panlongji, breached in the first year of Xianfeng (1851), flowing into Fengpei. At that time, the main current flooded, and the width of the river was more than twelve li. The old Yellow River has turned into a result of accumulated sediment and is more than ten feet higher than the newly formed river channel in Fengpei County. The terrain is even higher in the east with the two dams and the facing-water dam. Therefore, the Yellow River floods south to Panlongji and then enters the lake through the old Fengpei course. The nature of water is to flow downwards, which is dictated by the terrain. However, the people of Fengpei have a strange idea and want to divert the water upwards. They have even sent surveyors and police teams to measure the land along the two dams in Dangshan County and plan to send 20,000 laborers to block the Shayang River and excavate the two dams, so that the flooding Yellow River can be diverted through Dangshan and Xiaotong, avoiding harm to Fengpei. They also plan to mobilize the police and militia from the two counties, carrying ten thousand guns, to guard Dangshan, and are planning to set up a supervisor at Gaozhai and connect a telephone, and install electric lights to start work soon. The people of Xiaodang are running around sweating and are extremely indignant. They believe that along the old Yellow River course, towns and cities are densely populated. If the Fengpei diversion plan succeeds, all the towns and cities and transportation routes along the old course will be shaken and threatened every day. The two counties of Fengpei are treating their neighbors as moats and violating the nature of water, which will inevitably harm others for their own benefit. The one million people of Xiaodang can only take up arms to protect their lives and property, waiting for a fight. Now, the people of Tongshan County have also risen up in response and will unite with Xiaodang to oppose the Fengpei diversion plan. (11th Dispatch from the Central News Agency)

Liu Xiang Cables That the Sichuan-Tibet Border Earthquake Was Catastrophic

Unprecedented in Nearly a Century

(Nanjing) Liu Xiang cabled to Nanjing that the earthquake in the Songmao area has been verified. The entire area of Leixi has sunk into the ground, covering nearly a hundred li. Only three families in the parade ground are still alive. The rest, such as the Shawang and Camphor Tree factories, have been turned into a swamp. The scale of the loss is unprecedented in nearly a century. (11th Dispatch)

Sun Tonggang Arrives in Hangzhou

All Circles in Hangzhou Hold a Welcoming Meeting This Morning

(Hangzhou) Sun Tonggang visited Zhao Zhiyou at the Municipal Government at 4:30 PM and paid his respects to Lu Diping at the Provincial Government at 5:00 PM. Lu has scheduled a luncheon for Sun on the 12th. All circles will hold a welcoming meeting at the Provincial Party Headquarters on the morning of the 12th and invite him to give a speech. Sun will perform a flight demonstration in the sky over West Lake on the afternoon of the 12th. (11th Dispatch)

(Hangzhou) Sun Tonggang and Wang Zuwen flew to Jianqiao Aviation School Airport at 11:30 this morning. Hangzhou Mayor Zhao Zhiyou, Deputy Director of Aviation Cao Baoqing, Luo Zhentian of the provincial newspaper, and more than 300 representatives from all circles had already driven to Jianqiao from Hangzhou at 8:00 AM to welcome them. When Sun's plane landed, the crowd cheered. Female students Wu Zhengmin and Yuan Weiru presented flowers on behalf of all circles, and Luo Xiatian delivered a welcoming speech on behalf of all circles, praising Sun for crossing the ocean in a small plane with only 80 horsepower, which is a world first. Sun replied, (1) He hopes that Chinese people will manufacture airplanes in the future, (2) He hopes that in addition to training military aviation talent, they will also train transportation aviation talent, so that aviation can be popularized among the public and achieve the goal of aviation for the people and people for aviation. Sun told reporters that he took off from Shanghai at 10:15 this morning, and it took an hour and a quarter to reach here. Chen Wenlin accompanied him to the halfway point and then returned. He will stay in Hangzhou for a few days. In the future, he will fly to Anqing. After completing the nationwide flight, he will return to Germany or the United States to study aircraft manufacturing. Wang Zuwen also said that they plan to stay in Hangzhou for five or six days before flying again. All circles in Hangzhou have scheduled a welcoming meeting at the Provincial Party Headquarters on the morning of the 12th, a flight demonstration in Hangzhou at noon on the 12th, and a visit to the Aviation School and Aviation Office on the 13th, followed by a one- or two-day tour of the lake. (11th Dispatch from the Central News Agency)

Workers Laid Off by the Tianjin Bao Cheng Yarn Factory Petition

The Authorities Are Mediating

(Tianjin) After the labor dispute at the Bao Cheng Yarn Factory was mediated by the party and government authorities, the factory resumed work on a two-shift system on the evening of the 10th, laying off more than 600 workers. On the 11th, the laid-off workers petitioned the party headquarters, demanding (1) the payment of wages during the work stoppage, (2) layoffs must comply with the Factory Law, and (3) a travel allowance of five yuan per person. The factory responded with (1) a work stoppage wage of 2.5 yuan per person, (2) complete agreement, and (3) four yuan per person. The workers considered it insufficient and gathered at the Municipal Party Headquarters, not dispersing until night. Security forces have been mobilized to maintain order, and mediation is still underway. (11th Dispatch)

The United States and Japan Invite Britain to Participate in a Three-Power Naval Conference

To Revise the Washington and London Treaties

Japan Is Carefully Studying Countermeasures

(London) The "Daily Mail" today reported that the United States and Japan have decided to invite Britain to participate in a new three-power conference to revise the Washington and London Naval Treaties. The newspaper stated that after Japan recently protested President Roosevelt's decision to implement a shipbuilding program costing 47 million pounds, the US and Japanese governments exchanged notes and made this decision. (11th Reuters Dispatch) (Nanjing) According to diplomatic sources, the United Kingdom, the United States, and Japan are vigorously expanding their armaments, and the situation on the Pacific coast is becoming increasingly tense. Although the Japanese government is outwardly maintaining calm, it is actually deeply fearful. In order to ease this sharp confrontation, the Japanese diplomatic authorities have used diplomatic means and, as a result, have obtained the agreement of the United States to convene a three-power conference in the Pacific at a suitable location to discuss all major issues between the United States, the United Kingdom, and Japan. Our diplomatic authorities are paying close attention to this news. (11th Dispatch)

◆◆◆◆◆◆◆◆◆◆◆◆◆◆◆◆◆◆

London Officials Deny

(London) Various newspapers report that Washington and Tokyo have decided to invite Britain to participate in a new naval conference, but British officials have firmly denied this. (11th Havas Dispatch)

◆◆◆◆◆◆◆◆◆◆◆◆◆◆◆◆◆

(Tokyo) It is reported that Japan does not want to cancel the Washington Naval Treaty, but the Asahi Shimbun reports that there is a growing movement within naval circles arguing that Japan should declare that it cannot participate in any new naval agreement according to the existing ratio. The Hochi Shimbun predicts that Japan will suggest to the signatory countries of the Washington and London Treaties early next year that a preparatory meeting should be held before the Second Washington Conference in 1935. The Hochi Shimbun also states that Japanese naval personnel are strongly demanding equality in naval armaments. The Kokumin Shimbun speculates that Japan will propose the complete abolition of warships. (11th Reuters Dispatch)

(Tokyo) Regarding countermeasures for the Second Washington Naval Disarmament Conference in 1935, the Army, Navy, and Foreign Ministries will hold their second meeting this Thursday to prepare. On that day, they will further discuss the Washington and London Treaties from a legal perspective. The issue is the relationship between the validity periods of the two treaties and the 1935 conference. Although the Washington Treaty allows any signatory country to issue a notice of termination, it remains in effect for two years after the notice. If there is no notice of termination, it remains in effect for two years after it expires. Conversely, the London Treaty only stipulates that a conference should be convened in 1935 to revise the Washington Treaty. If no conference is convened or if it ends in failure, it expires at the end of 1936. However, the provisions on battleships and aircraft carriers contained in the London Treaty are also contained in the Washington Treaty and continue to exist. Since the validity periods of the two treaties are different, Japan must carefully study its countermeasures. Although the Washington Treaty allows for a notice of termination, it remains in effect for two years. Therefore, from the end of 1936 until the treaty is terminated, any agreement on the determination of military strength, no matter what form it takes, is insignificant in this sense, so the theory of the notice of termination is not worth emphasizing. However, it is worth noting that there are those who advocate issuing a strong notice to participating countries in a suitable period before the 1935 conference, stating that Japan cannot agree to the agreement on the strength of its military forces under the existing naval treaty, which can achieve the same effect as a notice of termination. (11th Den-tsu Dispatch)

Japan Is Building Airfields in the North

Aiming at Operations Against Russia and the United States

(Tokyo) The Japanese military believes that the air defense at the northern end is insufficient, and it is reported that it is secretly and actively planning to build three major airfields in Sakhalin, the Kuril Islands, and Hokkaido. The locations are reportedly Higashishirikori in Sakhalin, Shumushu in the Kuril Islands, and Nemuro in Hokkaido. In addition to building air force bases in these three places, it is also planned to open commercial aviation routes: (1) from Tokyo via Aomori, Nemuro, to Shumushu, a distance of 2,100 kilometers; (2) from Tokyo via Aomori, Sapporo, to Higashishirikori, a distance of 1,370 kilometers. It is reported that in the illegal negotiations on the Sino-Eastern Railway, the Japanese military advocated forcibly seizing it, so the future of the negotiations is full of twists and turns. Even if a satisfactory resolution is reached, there are still many difficulties in Russian-Japanese relations. According to the Japanese military's speculation, Russia has already signed non-aggression treaties with various Western European countries and is also mobilizing large armies to gather on the Russian-Manchurian border, under the command of Red Army Commander-in-Chief Moloshenov, conducting large-scale exercises of the Red Army. The United States is also seizing the opportunity to get closer to Russia and intends to buy the Kamchatka Peninsula as an air force base. Russia also wants to use American capital to develop the Maritime Province to curb Japan's northward policy. Japan believes that the world situation is gradually becoming unfavorable to it, so it wants to urgently build airfields for the air defense of the northern end. It is reported that the capitalists who contracted the project, under the guidance of the military and the Aviation Investigation Committee of the Ministry of Communications, have gone north to prepare for construction. (11th Chinese United Press Dispatch)

Huge Military Budget

Araki Bargains with the Finance Minister

(Tokyo) As a result of negotiations between the Japanese military and the Ministry of Finance, Finance Minister Takahashi has agreed that military spending takes precedence over everything else. In the budget for the next fiscal year, after deducting the military personnel needed for military spending, the remaining financial resources will be distributed to the heads of the various provinces. However, the total amount of new military spending has reached 840 million yuan. The new expenditures planned by the Japanese Ministry of Finance are around 700 million yuan. If this is the case, it will not be enough to cover all the military spending. Although the Ministry of Finance has agreed to Araki's principle, there are still many twists and turns ahead. According to Finance Minister Takahashi, this kind of problem cannot be discussed privately and should be submitted to the cabinet for discussion and decision. (11th Chinese United Press Dispatch)

(Tokyo) After the meeting between Army Minister Araki and Finance Minister Takahashi, the main problem in Japanese political circles has shifted to the military expenditure issue. The National Alliance today issued an opinion stating that the national defense expenditure should accept the demands of the military in such an urgent autumn of internal and external circumstances. Whatever the military needs, they should accept it. As for the financial resources, they should be paid for entirely with public bonds, which is perfectly acceptable. However, this expenditure should be managed with special accounting. (11th Chinese United Press Dispatch)

(Tokyo) The central issue of the Japanese government's budget for the next fiscal year is how to handle military spending. Of the 1.3 billion yuan of the total amount of new budgetary requests from various provinces, 370 million yuan are from the Army Ministry and 430 million yuan are from the Navy Ministry, totaling 800 million yuan, which accounts for more than 60% of the entire budget. The Accounting Bureau of the Ministry of Finance, which examines the budget, attaches great importance to this matter and has decided to start by reviewing the budget of the Navy Ministry. As for the Army, Interior, Agriculture, and Commerce Ministries, the authorities in charge of the Ministry of Finance are concerned about the future due to financial difficulties and plan to greatly reduce the budgets requested by the various provinces. However, the authorities in charge of the Army and Navy require all the funds to implement the national defense plan and future war plans. Therefore, the conflict between the military and financial authorities will inevitably intensify. Whether the two sides can compromise depends on the attitude of the military, because the military is in a passive position regarding the budget issue. Army Minister Araki's meeting with Finance Minister Takahashi on the 9th was the preliminary battle to resolve the military expenditure issue. As for the Navy, its importance to the internal and external situation is even greater than that of the Army, and it is concerned about the budgetary guidelines of the Ministry of Finance. The meeting between Navy Minister Osumi and Finance Minister Takahashi will be realized soon. However, ministers of the military and finance hope for a political solution to the military expenditure issue. Because the budget request for the next fiscal year is too large, it seems difficult to succeed. Now, both the military and the economy are serious due to the extraordinary situation and have special characteristics. To satisfy one, the other must be sacrificed. It is quite clear that this matter has a significant impact on Japan. How this problem will be resolved will be decided by the cabinet, so the results of the meeting between the finance minister and the military ministers can only be used as reference materials for the financial authorities, and it seems difficult to reach a complete consensus. The Japanese government's budget problem for the next fiscal year, which is centered on military spending, will inevitably be a fairly profound political conflict in the future. (11th Nippon Dempo Dispatch)

Hugh McMurray Is Appointed as Envoy to Small Neighboring Countries of Russia

Specializing in Collecting Information on Soviet Russia

A Prelude to the Restoration of Relations Between the United States and Russia

(Washington) Hugh McMurray, former US Minister to China, was today appointed by US President Kennedy as Minister to Latvia, Lithuania, and Estonia. It is generally believed that this is a prelude to his appointment as Ambassador to Russia after the restoration of relations between the United States and Russia in the future. McMurray will leave for his post immediately, and it is reported that he will work with the Minister to Sweden to investigate the economic and political situation of Soviet Russia to provide a reference for the US President's decision on the issue of recognition. The US Embassy in Sweden was previously ordered to investigate the current situation of Soviet Russia, but these three embassies are closer to Russia. The main reason for McMurray's appointment today is probably this. McMurray is currently a professor at Johns Hopkins University and there has been no news of his return to public service recently. Now he suddenly accepts the mission to these three small countries, and there is no other reason besides this. McMurray has served in China, Russia, and Japan, first as secretary of the Russian Embassy, then as secretary of the Japanese Embassy, and finally as Minister to China. He is familiar with the situation in Russia and the Far East, and it is most appropriate for him to be stationed in Moscow. Otherwise, the United States has neither large-scale trade nor important diplomatic issues with these three Baltic countries, so there is no need to use retired senior officials. However, the State Department and the White House have made no comment on this move, saying that there is no news on the issue of Soviet Russia. (10th Nationalist Electric)

This Year's League of Nations Assembly

As a Prelude to the Disarmament Conference

Election of Three Non-Permanent Council Members

(Geneva) The League of Nations Executive Council is scheduled to meet on September 22nd, and the League of Nations Assembly on September 25th. The agenda for this year's Assembly includes reports from the World Economic Conference and various other reports on purely technical matters, such as transportation, hygiene, opium trafficking, child protection, intellectual cooperation, and slave trade. The Disarmament Conference is scheduled to reconvene on October 16th, so the disarmament issue is not within the scope of the Assembly's discussions. However, according to usual practice at each League of Nations Assembly, there will be an open discussion of the Secretary-General's report. It is unknown whether speakers will touch upon the disarmament issue during such discussions. Even if there is no open discussion in the Assembly, the world's most pressing issue today is none other than disarmament. How can the Assembly not touch upon this serious issue? In short, even if the Assembly's debates and actions do not involve such issues, the Assembly's greatest concern will certainly be current political issues. This fourteenth League of Nations Assembly will serve as a prelude to the October 16th Disarmament Conference. This is almost certain. Regarding the organization of the Executive Council, this year's Assembly will elect three non-permanent representatives to the Executive Council to replace Guatemala, Norway, and Ireland, whose terms have expired. The Assembly will also accept Portugal's proposed new system, so this year the Executive Council representatives will expand to fifteen. The seat occupied by Japan in the Executive Council will be left vacant until the end of the two-year period, as the Covenant stipulates that a member state's declaration of withdrawal is only effective after two years. (Havas Dispatch, 11th)

Rumors of Soviet Russian Shipbuilding

Japan Angered by British Machinations

The Tokyo Hochi Shimbun reported on the 6th that the Soviet Russian government recently ordered four 7,000-ton cruisers equipped with elite cannons and one 3,800-ton ocean-going cruiser from Italian shipyards. All ships will be deployed in the Pacific Ocean. The Navy Ministry (Japan) was shocked by this information. In addition to investigating the truth, naval authorities believe that these rumors are entirely the work of Britain. The Soviet Russian government's warship construction plan is intended by British imperialists to stimulate the Japanese military and incite the deterioration of Japanese-Soviet relations. Britain is engaging in this inflammatory behavior because the Japanese military views the Red Army in Russian territory as a threat to Japan. Furthermore, Japan has always disliked the navigation of Soviet Russian fishing boats in the ocean. Therefore, Britain fabricated the story of warship construction for use in the Sea of Japan, intending to worsen Japanese-Soviet relations. Moreover, since Japan occupied Manchuria, Britain has long been wary of the expansion of the Japanese empire. Therefore, Britain greatly desires a conflict between Japanese policy and the Soviet Union or the United States. However, Japan's overseas expansion requires the investment of huge amounts of capital, so it must seek to dump goods to make up for the shortfall. As Japanese goods are sharp and aggressively infiltrating Britain and British colonies, Britain is very jealous and is trying to undermine the possibility of a peaceful policy in the contentious issues between Japan and Russia, so Britain can profit from it.

Soviet Russia's Large Aircraft "Heavenly City" to be Completed Soon

Equipped Like a City

Capable of Carrying Over Seventy Passengers (Moscow) The "Heavenly City" being built by Soviet Russia is about to be completed. "Heavenly City" is the name of the aircraft, and its size is the world's largest. It can carry seventy passengers and six crew members. It has a cinema, a printing house, a shortwave radio station, and a sky advertising area (projecting advertisements into the clouds). Its layout is like a city. The aircraft is a monoplane with a wingspan of 180 feet, equipped with eight engines, with approximately 4,000 horsepower. Its speed can reach 110 miles per hour. This aircraft will be the "flagship" of the Gorky Flying Squadron and will have its first test flight early next year. (Reuters)

Puppet Organization Cracks Down on Workers Entering the Country

(Dalian) It is reported that experts from the South Manchuria Railway, together with the Puppet Government authorities, are currently planning a method for laborers within Manchuria to have their fingerprints recorded. The purpose is to identify workers who leave and return, so that others cannot impersonate workers to enter the country. In the future, the entry of workers will be greatly restricted, and unemployed workers who are permanent residents in Manchuria will be utilized. It is estimated that there are currently 500,000 to 600,000 laborers in Manchuria, mostly recently from Shandong. About 120,000 of them are currently serving in national construction projects. Many workers come here in the spring and return to their hometowns in Shandong in the autumn. Officials claim that bandits often mix among the workers entering the country. (Reuters Dispatch, 11th)

Bovine Plague in Heilongjiang Province

Thousands of Deaths, Relief Efforts Exhausted

Carcasses Thrown into Nen River, Plague Spreads

(Dalian) Local Japanese newspapers report that the Manchu-Russian herdsmen in Heilongjiang Province have suffered many deaths recently due to the spread of bovine plague. Several thousand cattle have also died. Although the Puppet Ministry of Industry, in cooperation with medical experts from the South Manchuria Railway, has been working together to provide relief, the plague is still severe. In some places, almost all cattle have died. Thirty Manchus and about ten Russians who accompanied Japanese doctors to inspect the bovine plague were infected and died. But it is now believed that the total number of deaths should be more than this. About 2,000 cattle died along the Nen River, and their bodies were mostly thrown into the river, so the spread of the plague is extremely rapid in the lower reaches. (Reuters Dispatch, 11th)

Nazi Party's Broadcast Propaganda

Havas Dispatch, Berlin, 11th Some sources say that Austrian Prime Minister Dollfuss is now considering a policy of rapprochement with Germany to ease relations between the two countries. Naval Court Concludes Trial of the May 15th Incident

Prosecutor Argues for Sentencing

Koga and Three Others Sentenced to Death

Sixty Thousand Petitions for Leniency

China United News Agency, Tokyo, 11th: The naval perpetrators of the May 15th Incident were tried again this morning at 9:00 AM at the Yokosuka Naval Court. Prosecutor Yamamoto stood up to present his argument for sentencing. Yamamoto's argument lasted for more than three hours, until an 11:00 AM recess. China United News Agency, Tokyo, 11:00 AM: This was the 20th public trial of the naval perpetrators of the May 15th Incident. At 8:30 AM, there were 25 spectators. After the court convened at 9:00 AM, Prosecutor Yamamoto stood up to present his argument, stating that his argument was not subject to any interference and was entirely based on his own free opinion. The motives of the defendants were to eliminate the harm of political parties and financial cliques. There is no doubt that the defendants were correct in their assertions of corruption in the world, but the defendants also admitted that they had insufficient understanding of various facts. As for the right and wrong of various objective facts, it should be left to the judgment of the world. The defendants believed that only direct action could save the country from decline. This subjective argument was indeed dominated by the passion of youth, and they lost their fair judgment. There are understandable reasons for the defendants' feelings. However, from the perspective of national order, direct action is regrettable. The defendants conspired to murder, and according to the provisions of the Army Criminal Law, each is to be sentenced as follows: Navy Lieutenant Koga Kiyoshi, Navy Lieutenant Mikami Taku, and Reserve Navy Lieutenant Kuroiwa Isamu are sentenced to death. Navy Ensign Murayama Kakuji, Navy Lieutenant Nakamura Yoshio, and Navy Lieutenant Yamagishi Hiroshi are sentenced to life imprisonment. Navy Ensign Ito Kameki, Navy Ensign Ooba Haruo, and Navy Lieutenant Hayashi Masayoshi are sentenced to six years of imprisonment. Tsukano Michio is sentenced to three years of imprisonment.

Dentsu News Agency, Yokosuka, 11th: After the stern sentencing plea by Prosecutor Yamamoto in the naval court-martial regarding the May 15th Incident, the court adjourned at 11:01 AM and reconvened at 1:00 PM to begin the defense. First, Special Defense Counsel Captain Asada stated the following from a military perspective: Lieutenant Mikami and I were also classmates in the same class and vowed to be comrades-in-arms for the life and death of the country. These friends and relatives, seeing the clouded state of the imperial nation, transcended life and death to try to govern it. Although they are criticized for disrupting military discipline, they are determined to eliminate the dark clouds of depression and to summon a bright Showa Restoration to clarify the imperial way. Therefore, this sentiment has been the spirit of these people for eleven years and is well known to us. The reason is that the cabinet that assists His Majesty the Emperor has turned political parties into toys, and revealed policies of "selling dog meat under the banner of a sheep's head" to deceive the people. Moreover, its scandals are countless, such as the railway scandal of former Railway Minister Ogawa and former Education Minister Kobayashi, the sale of awards by the Director-General of the Honors Bureau of Amakasa, and the Tokyo municipal scandal. In addition, when concluding the London Naval Treaty, the authorities in the government clearly violated the supreme command, causing young officers to become extremely angry and determined to consolidate national defense. Captain Asada concluded his argument at 3:15 PM, and the court was adjourned.

Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 11th: Matsuda, Secretary-General of the Minseito Party, said of the argument for sentencing of the naval defendants that the logic was correct, the arguments were pure, and there was no need to say more, like drawing legs on a snake. Dentsu, Yokosuka, 11th: Regarding the naval defendants in the May 15th Incident, the argument for sentencing will be made soon. As of the 10th, Presiding Judge Takasu and other related judges had received as many as 60,000 petitions for leniency, only those transferred by the Navy Ministry. Among them was a petition written in blood on a handkerchief by Kojima Katsuya (15), a student at Doushi Kaisei Middle School. Other letters from all over the country requesting leniency also came like snowflakes, moving the presiding judge Takasu and other related judges considerably.

China United News Agency, Tokyo: Dr. Honda, President of Tohoku Imperial University in Japan, is a well-known scholar for his research on Japanese steel. Harbin Correspondence: The East China Republic has recently been actively seeking military expansion. The National Defense Army has completed two divisions, with approximately 84,000 personnel. ＝A Total of Seven Sites Have Been Mined＝

＝More Than Thirty Japanese Technicians＝

＝More Than Two Hundred Jin of Gold Extracted Daily＝

Tianjin Correspondence: After the four northeastern provinces were occupied by the Japanese, they separately exploited the mineral resources in various places. Since the Lugouqiao Incident, we have long expected that the Japanese would covet the world-renowned gold mines in northern Hebei and the rich coal mines along the Great Wall, with a view to exploiting our treasures and using them to build aggressive forces. Before the Tanggu Truce was signed, we heard that the Japanese and puppets had jointly organized a so-called "Japanese-Manchu Gold Mining Company" and dispatched technicians and workers to carry out surveys in Miyun, Zunhua, and Xinglong. Although most of the war zone has been recovered by us, the gold mine areas are still under continued occupation. According to people who have recently arrived from Zunhua, the gold mines in northern Hebei are best in Zunhua and Xinglong counties. Although Zunhua has been nominally recovered, in reality, eighty villages north of the Great Wall have not been recovered. Even the Daoliushui gold mine in the Malanyu area, located within the Great Wall, is still under the control of the Japanese army. I once tried to sneak into the gold mining site for an investigation and learned that the gold mining joint-stock company organized by the Japanese and puppets currently has seven mine shafts in the territory of Dushan, Xinglong, and Zunhua counties. There are a total of more than thirty Japanese technicians, more than ten puppet supervisors, and approximately seven hundred gold mining workers. A total of two hundred thirty to forty jin of gold can be mined from the seven sites every day. Among them is a small portion of placer gold, but the quality is exceptionally rich. Since mining began at the end of June, it has caused a sensation among the Japanese and puppet officials and people, who believe this is a sign of wealth and strength. A light railway has been built from the mining area to the Great Wall, and cars can be driven arbitrarily up and down the Great Wall. According to the people in the four counties of northern Hebei, who have strong solidarity and sufficient self-defense capabilities, the local authorities in North China once planned to jointly run the gold mines by officials and merchants and organized the Northern Hebei Gold Mining Company. The people of each county believed that the gold mines in these counties were the only way for all the people in the area to live in the future. They repeatedly jointly opposed it, and the officials planned to change it to official supervision and merchant management, which was also opposed by the county people. However, the county people themselves did not have this economic power. As a result, the mining plan was never implemented due to the preparations of the people in each county and the expression of armed opposition as a backer. Now, the mining rights have been seized by the Xun ethnicity, but there has been no expression of any kind from the people of the counties, presumably because they have been suppressed by the iron hooves of the Japanese army. (September 9th)

He Jian Reports on the Situation of Bandit Suppression in the Western Route

＝The First Column Guards the West Bank of the Gan River＝

＝The Second Column's Actions Are Relatively Slower＝

＝The Third Column Has Recovered Damushan Mountain＝

Changsha Correspondence: The Western Route General Headquarters was established on June 1st. The headquarters of the First, Second, and Third Columns under its command were also successively formed in June. It has been more than two months since then. Regarding the progress of bandit suppression, according to He Jian's report at the expanded memorial week of the party, government, and military, it is roughly as follows:

(Bandit Area Situation) The bandit situation on the Western Route Army's side is roughly divided into two types: main bandits and scattered bandits. The main bandits are the so-called Red Army, originally two groups led by Kong Hechong and Li Tianzhu (now led by Xiao Ke). Each group has approximately 10,000 people, with a maximum of approximately 5,000 to 6,000 guns, and a small number of machine guns and mortars. Kong's bandits have a main force of approximately 7,000 to 8,000 people, stationed in the Xiaoyuan, Paibu, Gao Village, and Xikeng areas on the border of Pinglu in eastern Hunan and Tonggu and Wanzai in western Jiangxi. Another group of approximately 3,000 to 4,000 people is stationed in the Damushan and Huanglongshan areas on the border of Chongyang, Tongcheng, Puqi, Yangxin, and Dazhi in southern Hubei. Xiao's bandits have a main force stationed in various areas of Yongxin, Lianhua, and Ninggang in southwestern Jiangxi. The above two groups of bandits use their lairs as bases and constantly harass various places. Scattered bandits are the so-called guerrillas, red guards, young pioneers, and other miscellaneous bandit units. These scattered bandits are often scattered in fixed areas, killing, arson, robbing, scouting news, and delivering documents, specializing in assisting the activities of the main bandits. There are a large number of people scattered in the border areas of western Jiangxi, southern Hubei, and eastern Hunan, arbitrarily harassing them. Their organization is very strict and is all ruled by the so-called Soviet governments at all levels. Most of the people in the bandit areas are banditized, especially in Yongxin, Lianhua, and Ninggang in southwestern Jiangxi, where banditization is the deepest. When our army enters, they often gather to resist or use the scorched earth policy to hinder the activities of our army, which greatly increases the difficulty of our army's suppression.

Suppression Status

(1) The First Column is responsible for suppressing bandits in the Yongxin, Lianhua, and Ninggang area in southwestern Jiangxi. Wang Dongyuan and Chen Guangzhong's divisions have already recovered Lianhua and Ninggang. All the scattered bandits east of Chaoyougui have also been cleared. The above places are currently organizing the masses and handling all local aftermath matters to seek fundamental cleansing. Around August 11th, Xiao's bandits, seeing that the First Column was using a steady and gradual method of eliminating bandits, were extremely panicked and used its main force of approximately four regiments with four to five thousand guns, ambushing near the Meihua Mountains in western Jiangxi (hundreds of li in length) to prevent our Peng Division from advancing. The Peng Division successively defeated them, killing more than 1,500 bandits, seizing dozens of guns, and capturing many prisoners. Our army also suffered minor casualties. After being hit, the bandits fled to the vicinity of Dafuping on the border between Xia County and Ninggang, where they were again severely attacked by the Wang Division. They are now fleeing towards Yongxin, and our army is tracking and pursuing them. The most important task of the First Column is to guard the west bank of the Gan River. Now the fortifications are strong and the troops are strong. In fact, the main bandits in eastern Jiangxi cannot cross the river at present. (2) The Second Column is responsible for suppressing bandits in the northwestern Jiangxi area. I am concurrently serving as the commander of the column, and the actions are relatively slower because the transfer of various troops takes time. Now the transfer has been completed and we are besieging the bandit troops. Seeing our army approaching, the bandits are fleeing in all directions. Yesterday, I received a telegram from Tao Brigade Commander of the 19th Division, Liujiang, reporting that four to five hundred armed bandits had sneaked into Liuyang and attacked Sunjiaduan. They have been defeated, killing fifty to sixty bandits. There are also more than 1,000 pseudo-18 armed bandits who attacked Huangfang and are confronting the Li Security Regiment and the Volunteer Army guarding our blockhouse. Our side has dispatched troops to sandwich them. The scattered bandits in other places have not yet had any riots, and the local area is still quiet. The scattered bandits in Pingxiang will also be cleared in the shortest time. The car from Pingxiang to Nanchang can pass without hindrance. (3) The Third Column is responsible for suppressing bandits in southern Hubei. The divisions under the command of Commander Chen's column set off separately on the 10th of last month to besiege the Damushan bandit lair. The mountain peaks are extremely high, and the mountain range is very large, stretching for more than 600 li. Our army is making efforts to suppress them, and has successively destroyed many bandit lairs, killing more than a thousand bandits, seizing dozens of guns and four mortars, and capturing more than 400 bandits alive. On the 29th of last month, the mountain was completely recovered. Most of the bandits have been defeated, and the remnants are now disintegrating into zero to try to survive. Commander Chen's column has ordered the local garrison to strictly clear them and handle the aftermath to eliminate their roots. Southern Hubei is expected to be completely cleared in the near future. In addition to the above-mentioned bandit suppression situation, there are also two things about local security. (1) A thousand or so of He Long's bandits sneaked into Wangjiachang, Songzi, Hubei, and the border of Hunan a few days ago, and the area of Jinfeng was uneasy. Our corps have rushed to suppress them, and He's bandits have fled to Hefeng. The main force of He's bandits stationed in the border area of Laifeng Longshan is currently being besieged by our 34th Division and the armies of Hubei Province, and it is not difficult to defeat them. (2) Chen Wu's department in Zhijiang was disarmed by our Li and Chen brigades on the 25th of last month. Chen Wu was taken advantage of by villains when the Guangdong and Guangxi armies were preparing to enter Hunan and resist Japan last time, thinking that there would be some changes in Hunan, so he dared to take the opportunity to rebel in western Hunan. When the provincial army entered the suppression, Chen's department entrenched in Zhijiang County, relying on its dangerous and solid defenses, hoping to wait for the situation to change. The provincial army had planes and artillery, and it was not difficult to bomb them, but because of the civilians in the city, they could not bear to bomb them. The siege lasted for nearly two months, and fortunately, the officers and soldiers worked hard to climb the city and recaptured Zhicheng on the 25th of last month. Most of the rebel army has been disarmed, and Chen has only led a small number of rebel soldiers to escape. They are currently being hunted down. In addition, there is a small group of bandits in Huaihua, and Zhou Yucheng's department has fled to the border of Mayang. It is also reported that Yan Zhongru is collecting bandits in western Hunan. Li is now dispatched to Hongjiang to clear the remnants of the bandits and handle the aftermath. It is expected that the order in western Hunan will be completely restored. (September 8th)

Weng Zhaoyuan Appointed Commander of Fuzhou City Defense

The Public Security Bureau's Lianjia Committee is Also Established

Fuzhou Correspondence: Recently, due to the tense military situation of bandit suppression in northern Fujian, the hearts of the people in the provincial capital have suddenly become turbulent, and the money market has become very tight. The Pacification Headquarters specially appointed Weng Zhaoyuan as the commander of the city defense, placing the 61st Division's Wu Kangnan Regiment of the 19th Route Army and the Sun Lanquan Regiments of Chen Ren's Replacement Division under his command. Weng immediately set up a department in the Donghu barracks on the 5th and began to work. The Lianjia Committee organized by the Public Security Bureau of the provincial capital was also established on the 5th. Qiu Zhaochen, the Director of the Public Security Bureau, was appointed as the chairman of the committee, and an order was issued that Lianjia offices should be established in all neighborhoods to prevent petty theft. The First Fleet Commander Chen Jiliang, led by six ships, also arrived in Fujian on the 5th. However, those who moved and relocated were still constantly on the road. Although the Pacification Headquarters, the Provincial Government, the City Defense Headquarters, and the Public Security Bureau of the provincial capital issued notices to stop them, they were still ineffective. Most of the various industries and commerce are in a state of stagnation. (September 7th)

Guangdong Army Deploys Defenses on the Fujian-Guangdong Border

＝Because the Fujian Bandits Invaded Yanping, the Situation is Tense＝

＝Li Yangjing Changes to Luofu Mountain for Recuperation＝

Guangzhou Correspondence: The Minxi Communist bandits have invaded Yanping again, and the Guangdong border defense is becoming increasingly tense. In addition to rushing to build border fortifications, bunkers, and trenches, the Southern Route Bandit Suppression Army has also added airfields in various places. At the moment, the project has been completed in order. The air force has the Fourth Team Xie Mang Department in Dongjiang, the Fifth Team Wu Jianwen Department, the Third Team Tao Zuode Department in southern Jiangxi, and the Second Team Ding Jixu Department in Beijiang. In order to increase the strength of the infantry in front, the headquarters ordered the artillery battalions of each army to rush to the front. After receiving the order, the troops departed from the province during the day. The Independent Third and Fourth Divisions stationed in Beijiang will transfer a portion of their troops to southern Jiangxi. The Wang Dinghua Regiment stationed in Dongjiang is also preparing to move to the Fujian-Jiangxi border during the day. Li Yangjing, the commander of the Third Army, was previously suspected by Chen Jitang of supporting Li Jishen, so he has been recuperating in the Yi Yangyuan. It has been eight months. In July, he left the garden for a while. Soon after, he moved to the Meihua Village outside the East Suburb. Recently, because the Mei Hua Village residence is close to the city area, he changed to Luofu Mountain, which borders Zengcheng Boluo in Dongjiang, for recuperation. He set off from the province on the 3rd of this month. Chen Jitang's Chief of Military Law Li Guocai, Deng Qingbiao, Director of the Rear Office of the Third Army, and his wife and children were traveling with him. In addition, there was a company of military police machine guns and a special service battalion of the Third Army for consolidation. When Li boarded the Guangzhou-Kowloon Railway, he first returned to his hometown of Dongbei Wangyuan, took a three-day rest, and then left for Luofu Mountain on the morning of the 6th. At noon, he arrived at Chongxu Temple at the foot of the mountain. After Li entered the mountain, all military affairs of the Third Army were temporarily presided over by Huang Zhiwen, commander of the Eighth Division. The position of commander of the Second Column was assumed by the Chief of Staff of the Third Army. All bandit suppression work was kept out of the way by Li, and it is strange that he had been recuperating for more than eight months. (September 6th)

Guangdong Provincial Bank Consolidates Central Bank Notes

All Central Bank Notes to Stop Registration on Schedule

Another Method of Returning Cash for Deposits is Formulated to Recover Central Bank Notes

Guangzhou Correspondence: The Central Bank notes of the former Guangdong Provincial Central Bank were stopped from circulation after the Central Bank was changed to the Provincial Bank. The Provincial Bank was responsible for registering the Central Bank notes and redeeming them on schedule. It has been eight months since it was handled, and the number of redemptions will be completed soon. Recently, in order to complete the handling as soon as possible, the Provincial Bank specially issued a notice to stop the registration of Central Bank notes, and another method for returning cash was formulated. The notice stated that the bank had decided to stop registering the one-yuan, five-yuan, fifty-yuan, and one-hundred-yuan Central Bank notes simultaneously from the 11th of this month to end the registration. Those who have already registered can still wait for the date and number to be compiled on a monthly basis and go to the Provincial Bank for verification and redemption. As the five-yuan Central Bank notes remain in the market in a large number, and the fifty-yuan Central Bank notes are also registered together with the five-yuan notes, in order to sort them out and complete the task as soon as possible, the bank has formulated the following methods for returning cash for five-yuan and fifty-yuan Central Bank notes: (1) In order to sort out the five-yuan and fifty-yuan Central Bank notes and shorten the verification and redemption period, the Provincial Bank will, in addition to verifying and redeeming them in the order of registration numbers, also hold five-yuan and fifty-yuan Central Bank note deposits, and regularly return cash to end the process quickly. (2) Anyone holding five-yuan and fifty-yuan Central Bank notes, whether they have been registered or not, may deposit them into this bank together with 50% of the value in five-yuan and fifty-yuan Central Bank notes and 50% in silver dollars. The bank will issue a receipt for the full amount as a silver dollar deposit, and the funds will be fully refunded in cash after a deduction of four months from the date of deposit. (3) When depositors deposit five-yuan and fifty-yuan Central Bank notes and silver dollars into this bank, they should fill out the seal and save it with the bank for verification when returning the cash. (4) The maximum total amount of deposits collected each day is provisionally set at 100,000 yuan for adjustment. (5) After this deposit expires, depositors may go to the bank to withdraw cash with proof at any time during the bank's business hours. There is no fixed deadline and no notice will be issued to solicit claims. (September 7th)

Quelling Remaining Defeated Soldiers in Anhui

=Local Authorities Handling Aftermath=

=Relief for Disaster Victims After Looting=

Correspondance from Bengbu: The routed soldiers from Henan Province led by Cheng Fan, who disturbed the Anhui region, have been driven back to Luyi County in Henan Province through the joint efforts of Henan and Anhui troops. Fuyang and Yingshang counties, which suffered severe devastation, are now gradually stabilizing. In the border areas of Guoyang and Mengcheng, the people were greatly alarmed and the local authorities were extremely tense due to the accumulated bandits among the routed soldiers who intended to intrude. The bandit group was then tracked and pursued by the troops suppressing the bandits and the security teams, and the bandits fled westward. According to the person in charge of the Provincial Security Office, the routed soldiers and accumulated bandits who recently harassed the Anhui region used the name of the Anti-Japanese Allied Army. Fortunately, with the cooperation of various troops, the bandits did not succeed. The remaining bandits staying in the Fuyang-Taihe region have been continuously suppressed and eliminated by Cheng Ziyi's unit of the Henan Security Detachment, Zu Xinzhai's 1st Regiment of the Anhui Provincial Security Team, and Ni Rongxian's 2nd Regiment. There are no longer any traces of bandits in the area. Luo Jingyou, the administrative inspector of the 7th District of Anhui Province, is currently comforting the displaced people and handling the aftermath. The relief commissioners sent by the Anhui Provincial Government and the Provincial Relief Association to Fuyang have also arrived and are currently engaged in investigating and distributing relief to the disaster victims after the looting. Jiang Yi, the director of the Changhuai River Police Bureau, who went to Hao County for inspection, returned to Bengbu by boat today (the 10th). According to him, the bandits in the Guoyang-Mengcheng area have all been scattered and will be completely quelled within days. (September 10th)

Shaanxi Disaster Areas Appeal for Relief

丨Serious Disaster Conditions in Various Counties丨

Correspondance from Xi'an: Shaanxi Province has suffered three severe floods in the past two months, especially the Wei River basin, which has been heavily affected. The summer harvest has already been poor in various counties, and the autumn crops have been washed away by the floods, leaving nothing behind. The situation is more serious than ever before. Now, the counties that have survived the disaster are sending urgent telegrams and letters requesting relief. The following are excerpts from the relief request telegrams and letters from Lintong, Fengxian, and other places:

Lintong

The Lintong County Party Affairs Guidance Office telegraphed the Provincial Relief Association on August 14th, stating that the county along the Wei River had suffered severe floods, requesting a large sum of money for emergency relief.

Fengxian

In Fengxian, on August 30th, at 4:00 PM, heavy rain fell, causing mountain streams to surge violently, reaching a height of about 30 feet. The floodwaters split into two streams, one flowing from the Telou River and the other flowing from Kuangouzi through Tougou, Ergou, and Sangou, all entering the Baishui River. Houses and utensils were completely submerged, and livestock were swept away by the current, resulting in significant deaths. Fertile land has been turned into rocky beaches and rivers. The devastation is so unprecedented and severe that it has set a new record for Fengxian. Emergency relief is urgently needed.

Dali

On August 8th, at 12:00 AM, the upstream waters of the Luo River surged violently, rising more than 10 feet high, overflowing in all directions. All the more than forty villages along the banks in the eastern, western, southern, and northern districts of the territory were turned into a watery expanse. The crops and autumn harvest were completely submerged.

Livestock and utensils were swept away by the current, and the collapse of houses and the loss of property are even more difficult to calculate. The plight of tens of thousands of disaster victims crying out for food is truly unbearable to hear. The Dali authorities, in their eagerness to provide relief, have temporarily set up a reception center. It is also reported that the county party headquarters and the county government have urgently requested the province to allocate a large sum of money to carry out relief efforts.

Bin County

From August 6th to 9th, the Jing River in Bin County rose sharply, with the width of the water level several times greater than that of the Yellow River. More than a hundred people were drowned, and several thousand mu of autumn crops along the river were completely submerged. The severity of the flood is many times greater than the droughts in recent years. It is reported that the county has submitted a report to the Provincial Government and the Relief Association, earnestly requesting relief.

Suide

The Suide County Magistrate recently submitted a report to Chairman Shao, Director Yang, Director Hu, Director Zhao, Director Ning, and the Provincial Relief Association, stating that the entire county had suffered severe floods and requesting emergency relief to save the disaster victims. He expressed his gratitude and awaited further instructions.

Long County

The Provincial Government recently received a report from the Long County Magistrate on the flood situation in the county, stating that in addition to finding ways to comfort and resettle the displaced, they requested a quick allocation of funds for relief.

Baoji

The Wei River in this county suddenly surged on August 8th, washing away all the crops. Good fields are covered with mud, and dozens of villages have been washed away. More than a thousand people have drowned, and the loss of autumn crops cannot be fully recorded.

Baocheng

In early August, there was a heavy rainstorm, and

mountain floods suddenly arrived, with water depths exceeding ten feet. Many people became victims of the waves. The documents, public goods, and clothing of the officials in the area were completely washed away. The crops in the entire area were submerged and withered, and houses collapsed, leaving the people without shelter. A detailed survey of the disaster situation is currently underway.

China Pavilion at the Chicago Exposition Completed

丨Opening on August 6th丨

Correspondance from Chicago: The public exhibition room in the southwest corner of the China Pavilion at the Chicago Exposition has been completed and opened on August 6th. The exhibits include ancient pottery, porcelain, brick carvings, and currency from the Three Dynasties, as well as educational materials and paintings. The Propaganda Committee of the Chinese Products Association also began giving lectures there on the same day. Lectures are held once a day at 6:00 PM, with most of the speakers being students from the University of Chicago. The daily topics are as follows: Sundays: Introducing the New China; Mondays: New Construction in China; Tuesdays: Sino-American Commercial Relations; Wednesdays: Chinese Family Life; Thursdays: Modern Chinese Women; Fridays: Old and New Education in China; Saturdays: China and the World. These lectures have been well-received by the audience since their inception. On August 9th, the representative of Japan's participation in the Chicago Exposition also attended the lecture and expressed great interest.

Songjiang

Compensation for the Tragic Death of Telephone Workers

Near the city's gunpowder bureau and the tax police officers' training institute, a broken electric light line was hanging down, resting on the telephone line, preventing it from functioning. The telephone company dispatched five technicians to repair it, and immediately notified the electric light company to close the section's circuit breaker to prevent danger. However, it was dark at the time, and the telephone workers mistakenly believed that the circuit breaker had been closed. As they started repairs, workers Chen Huigen and Wu Ahe were successively electrocuted and killed. The families of the deceased, especially the elderly and young, relied on the deceased for their livelihood. Hearing of the tragic death, they wailed in sorrow, and onlookers cried out for justice on their behalf. The telephone company held a shareholders' meeting yesterday to discuss compensation issues. According to regulations, each family will receive a funeral grant of one hundred yuan and six months' salary. However, after deducting the funeral expenses, the family will receive very little. Therefore, Zhu Jiuwang, the manager of the telephone company, contacted Manager Gong of the electric light company to request additional compensation to support the lives of the bereaved families. However, no results have been achieved yet.

Wuxi

Eight People Bitten by a Mad Dog

Mad dog attacks on people are frequently heard in this region. Any delay in treatment can be fatal. The harm they cause is terrifying. Lu Heshang, a resident of the Hua Dafang Village in Xin'an Township, District 13, is a butcher. The other day, he went to the Lu family in Yuantang Bridge to buy a large pig. As he was leaving, he suddenly saw a dog, completely black, baring its teeth and claws, jumping and roaring like thunder. It appeared mad. Lu was about to dodge, but it was too late. He was bitten in the foot, suffering a severe wound with blood gushing out. The next day, the mad dog ran to Qianbing Bridge and bit a Chen family child in the head. Then, it went to the Xue Dian Bridge area and bit people randomly. In total, eight people were bitten. The mad dog has now been killed by the villagers. The eight injured people will travel together to Langshan in Nantong for treatment.

Changzhou

Re-election of the Boy Scouts Council

The Wuyi Boy Scouts Council held a re-election meeting for directors on the 10th. Xue Digong, the provincial council supervisor, service member Li Guangdao, and nineteen others were present. Liu Guorong was publicly elected as the temporary chairman. As a result of the re-election, Zhou Shanbai, Liu Guorong, and Li Yusheng were elected as directors, and Mei Dasheng, Chen Yinyu, and Mei Guofang were elected as alternate directors. The temporary chairman, together with the supervisor, submitted the election results and the election ballots to the Jiangsu Provincial Council for review.

Villager Commits Suicide Due to Economic Pressure

Zhang Wuda, a villager from Xizhuang Township, District 7 of Wuyi, nearing sixty years of age, has been suffering from illness and economic difficulties. He planned to sell his fields, but no one inquired about them. He hanged himself the night before. The next morning, neighbors went inside to check on him and found him hanging naked by the side of the bed, already dead. Everyone was saddened by this.

Jiading

Abortion Leads to Death, Body Hidden in Ruined Shack

Chen Xiao, a carpenter from the Fan Chen residence northeast of Nanxiang in this county, has been a fugitive since being wanted for extortion and murder a few years ago. His wife, Zhang, aged twenty-nine, could not get used to sleeping alone after her husband left. She became intimate with a certain Jia from her clan and became pregnant after four months. Fearing her husband's condemnation upon his return, Jia took her to Shanghai for an abortion. Introduced by someone on the twenty-second of last month, they returned to Jinjia Village, northeast of Fangtai in this county, and commissioned the midwife Zhu Zhang to perform the procedure. First, she administered some kind of medication, followed by a surgical operation on the twenty-fourth, inserting some kind of bone instrument into her vagina to induce the fetus to descend. Chen Zhang cried out in pain and died. After causing the accident, Zhu Zhang and Jia buried the body in the fields at midnight. Their actions were spotted by a fisherman. Later, the corpse rotted, emanating a foul odor. Passersby inquired with the fisherman and learned the secret, which spread far and wide. Zhu Zhang then moved the body and buried it in a bean field elsewhere. The Fangtai Public Security Substation learned of the situation and detained Zhu Zhang's fourteen-year-old daughter, Caiying. Using certain methods, they obtained all the details. The county Public Security Bureau reported the matter to the county government. On the ninth, Investigator Zhang led officials to the site for an on-site examination. A child's foot was found in the deceased's lower body, proving that the deceased was indeed Chen Zhang and had died from injuries sustained during the abortion. The death certificate was immediately filled out, and burial arrangements were ordered. Zhu Zhang and Zhu Caiying were both taken into custody for interrogation.

Gaoyou

Patrol Officer Accused, Department Orders Investigation

Zhang Xiangling, the patrol officer of the 4th Public Security Substation in this county, was previously accused by citizens Wang Shoushan and others of illegal detention and fines, abuse of power, and harming the people. They requested that the county be ordered to remove him from his post and severely punish him. It is now heard that the Public Hearing Office has ordered the county government to conduct a thorough investigation and report back for review and action.

Police Team Accidentally Kills Fisherwoman

Several bandits suddenly arrived in Zhongzhuang, District 7 of the County School, demanding that the village raise 3,000 yuan within ten days and send it to the river crossing, or they would set the entire village on fire. The villagers were extremely alarmed and reported to the county government, which sent a police team to be stationed there. The other day, a small fishing boat was moored on the river below the village, with a mother and son on board. When the police team patrolled to that location, they asked about the boat. Unexpectedly, the fisherman's son answered "Brothers," leading the police team to suspect they were bandits and open fire. The bullets pierced the fisherman's son's leg and struck the fisherwoman in the abdomen. The fisherwoman died on the spot. How tragic!

Rugao

Major Flooding in Beikan Town

In Beikan, Rugao County, a hurricane suddenly struck on the night of the 6th, causing a sudden surge in the sea, with tremendous momentum. The residents of the area were awakened from their dreams and looked around. In an instant, the tide surged, as if galloping horses, and crossed the Fan Gong embankment, entering Beikan Town. In a moment, the place became a vast expanse of water, becoming a wetland. Only the thirty-odd households in Wan'erdun were not flooded. The losses were enormous. Today (the 8th), the storm has subsided, and the water is gradually receding. In addition to urgently telegramming the county government for relief, the local public office has strictly ordered the laborers to set up defenses to prevent the unexpected.

Jiashan

Robbery of Fishing Boat, Four Lives Shot

Luhu, where this county borders Wujiang, is a water town infested with bandits. Yesterday, a case of robbery and murder of four people occurred in Yinzi Village, south of the town. The victim was a Mr. Gu, who was a fisherman, living on his boat. Besides his wife, there were also his octogenarian mother and three-year-old child. Unexpectedly, yesterday they encountered a pirate ship, which blocked them, robbed them, and then shot and killed the Gu family, all four lives, abandoning the bodies on the shore, and sailing away.

Discussing County-Wide Grain Storage for Famine Relief

The county government, upon receiving instructions from the province to prepare for grain storage as a vital policy for famine relief, convened a county administrative meeting: (1) The first phase will require the solicitation of 70,042 shi of grain, to be completed within one month; (2) The shortfall of over 60,000 shi will be filled in two ways: first, converting the value of rice from district farmers into grain; second, each township office should independently store grain according to the population it serves; (3) Each mu of land will be assessed one sheng of dried grain, which can be substituted with brown rice. This will be collected by the township police and supervised by township citizens, borne by the property owners, and deducted from the tenants' rent payments.

Appealing for Reduction of Land Tax Surcharges

The various surcharges on land tax in this county, such as education, autonomy, construction, pest control, and water conservancy, are numerous and exceed the principal tax by more than half. Numerous requests for reduction have not only been denied, but this year, the cost of the security corps has increased by one jiao per mu, and the aviation donation for farmers has increased by two fen per yuan. Furthermore, the expenses for rural primary schools are also included in the collection of land tax. This county is a heavily taxed area, and with poor harvests and famine, the rural areas are bankrupt and cannot bear repeated burdens. Yesterday, citizens such as Jiang Shusen submitted separate petitions to the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Finance, and the provincial government, appealing for reduction to alleviate the people's distress.

Economic Hardship Forces Suicide

In Nancheng, this county, there was a Huai Bingwen, who was fifty-five years old. He had one son and one daughter. Besides his elderly wife, he also had his mother-in-law living with him. He used to run a sauce garden, but due to the business downturn in recent years, all the shops were cutting back, and Huai closed his business and returned home. From then on, his economic situation became more strained. As a last resort, he made a living as a street vendor. Due to his old age and declining strength, his meager earnings were barely enough. Yesterday, he was unable to make ends meet and asked relatives for a loan, but he was rejected. He panicked and decided on suicide. As expected, he hanged himself in the middle of the night when everyone was asleep. When he was discovered, he had already died. He had no money for a coffin or funeral. His wife had to beg for donations to purchase a coffin. How tragic!

Hangzhou

The Bizarre Case of the Beautiful Corpse and Jade Arm

The Yuehua Barber Shop at No. 77 Guanchiao Straight Street in Hangzhou was just opened last month. Yesterday morning (the 11th) at 8:00 AM, due to the need to install water pipes, the mason Wu Ziqing was digging a hole. Suddenly, half a foot below the ground, he discovered the arm of a female corpse, which had not rotted. Because the fingernails were very long, it was estimated that the body had been buried there for several years. The police learned of this and took the shop owner Yu Degui, the mason Wu Ziqing, and the landlord Chen Pinshan to the police station, where Officer Hong conducted an interrogation. It is still difficult to find clues in this bizarre corpse case.

Jiaxing

Remaining City Walls Offered for Tender at Reduced Price

The remaining city walls from the West Gate to the South Gate in Jiaxing are now being demolished in accordance with orders. The county construction department surveyed and measured the area and divided it into twenty-four sections, estimating the value for bidding. The County Construction Committee decided to solicit bids for demolition. Unexpectedly, at the opening of bids the other day, only seventeen sections passed. Contracts have already been signed and the demolition is being urged. The remaining sections that did not pass are now being re-offered for tender at a 10% discount off the original bid price due to the sharp drop in brick prices, as decided by the County Construction Committee yesterday. The reasons for the discount will be reported to the Construction Department for record.

On the evening of the 9th, in the Ren'an Yan area outside the South Gate, a guest merchant, Xia Changgui, suddenly used a kitchen knife in a small boat to slash at his guest, Chen Chuyi, removing a large piece of Chen's brain. Blood flowed non-stop, and Chen fell to the ground unconscious. Chen's wife, Jiang, cried loudly for help. By the time the villagers arrived after hearing the cries, Xia had already fled far away. Chen's wife has now reported to the county for an autopsy. The assailant's injuries are very serious, and there are concerns about his life.
