Local News

Two Aviators Left Shanghai Yesterday

Sun Tonggang Flew to Hangzhou at 10:00 AM Yesterday

Chen Wenlin Flew to Nanjing at 2:00 PM in the Afternoon

Separately Embarking on the Grand Mission of Circumnavigating the Country

Sun Tonggang, a young aviator who studied in Germany, left Shanghai yesterday morning at 10:00 AM after attending the naming ceremony of the five aircraft. Accompanied by his classmate Wang Zuwen, he flew his own aircraft from Hongqiao Airport to Hangzhou to continue his national flight. Chen Wenlin, the director of the Xiamen Naval Aviation Department, and Pan Dingxin, the head of the mechanical section, also flew the self-made Jiangque aircraft to Beijing at 2:25 PM yesterday afternoon, commencing the grand mission of flying around the country. This is welcomed by the people.

Sun's Departure from Shanghai

Before departing from Shanghai for Hangzhou, Sun Tonggang had originally planned to depart at 9:00 AM, but it was later changed to 10:00 AM. When Sun and his classmate Wang Zuwen arrived at Hongqiao Airport, Lin Wojiang, the Secretary-General of the Aviation Association, Xie Qi, the Director of the Consolidated Tax Bureau, Wang Yuanlong of the United Company, and his wife Tan Shaoji, as well as movie star Tan Xuerong, also arrived to see them off at the airport. Ms. Tan presented Sun with a bouquet of flowers, and the Star Film Company made a farewell film of Sun for commemoration. Sun then shook hands with each of the well-wishers, bidding them farewell. Amid the cheers, he flew the aircraft into the air, circled the field several times, repeatedly waving his hands, reluctant to leave, before heading south. At that time, Chen Wenlin, the director of the Naval Aviation Department, was test flying the Jiangque aircraft, which had been repaired. He also approached to shake hands with Sun before Sun boarded the aircraft. He then flew the aircraft, accompanying Sun for several circles around the field, seeing him off a distance. As Sun and Chen were departing at the same time to undertake the grand mission of circumnavigating the country, they made a passionate arrangement to meet in Fujian Province when the opportunity arose.

Sun and Wang's Conversation

When the reporter saw Sun and Wang off at the airport, he had the following conversation with them: (Q) Mr. Sun, how many days will you stay in Hangzhou? (A) About a week. (Q) What is your itinerary when you depart from Hangzhou for the national flight? (A) I will fly to Anqing, Hankou, Changsha, then back to Hankou, and then to Zhumadian, Zhengzhou, Luoyang, Xi'an, and directly to Lanzhou. From Lanzhou, I will turn back and fly to Bian, then to Baoding, Datong, Zhangjiakou, Suiyuan, and then to Beiping. After visiting the war zone in Beiping, I will fly to Tianjin and then directly back to Jinan. (Q) What are your plans after completing the national flight, sir? (A) To study aircraft manufacturing in Germany, which will take four years to graduate. According to Wang Zuwen, I will continue to help Mr. Sun complete the national flight to draw the attention of compatriots nationwide to national salvation and construction. After completing the flight, I may continue my studies or serve in the country. No decisions have been made yet. It is also learned that Mr. Sun has received enthusiastic assistance from all sides for this trip, so after several years, he will return to meet with the people in a grand undertaking to circumnavigate the world.

Chen and Pan Fly to Beijing

Chen Wenlin, the Director of the Xiamen Naval Aviation Department, and Pan Dingxin, the head of the mechanical section, departed from Xiamen on July 20th, flying the self-made Jiangque aircraft. On the 25th, they arrived in Shanghai via Fuzhou, Wenzhou, and Nanjing. The original engine of the aircraft had 85 horsepower, which was not suitable for long-distance flight, so it was replaced with a 120-horsepower engine in Shanghai. The delay lasted until now, more than a month. It was not until the day before yesterday that the installation was completed. Chen Wenlin, the Director of the Naval Aviation Department, test-flew at Hongqiao Airport at about 10:00 AM yesterday, and flew Sun Tonggang to near Jiaxing before returning to Shanghai, landing at Hongqiao Airport, very satisfied. Then, at 2:25 PM, he officially took off with the head of the mechanical section, Mr. Pan Dingxin, leaving Shanghai for Beijing. Those who went to Hongqiao Airport to see them off included Li Shijia, the Vice Minister of the Navy, Zeng Yijing, the Director of the Naval Aircraft Manufacturing Department, and many of Chen's relatives and friends.

Planned Itinerary

Chen Wenlin originally planned to travel with Sun Tonggang, but since their itineraries are different, he decided to fly separately. Chen

estimates that he will be able to reach Nanjing at about 4:00 PM yesterday afternoon. This morning, he will take off from Beijing and go directly to Beiping. He will stay in Beiping for about three days before returning to Shanghai via Tianjin and Qingdao, and then returning to Xiamen via Zhejiang. He will then fly to South China. The reporter met Chen Wenlin at the airport yesterday, who said that after arriving in Beijing this time, he will stay for one day. The next morning, he will depart from Beijing, passing through Xuzhou, Jinan, and Tianjin, to reach Beiping. Then, he will return to Shanghai from Beiping via Tianjin and Qingdao. The estimated itinerary is about one week. At that time, he will still land at Hongqiao Airport, stay in Shanghai for one day, and then go south through Hangzhou, Ningbo, and Wenzhou to return to Xiamen. He will then fly to Shantou, Hong Kong, Guangzhou, Wuzhou, and other places. After reaching Liuzhou, he will turn back and fly to Hankou, turning to Shanghai along the Yangtze River, and then returning directly to the Xiamen Naval Aviation Department to complete the national flight plan. After success, he will build a larger aircraft and then make a round-the-world flight.

Regular Inspection of Disaster Areas by the Yellow River Flood Relief Committee

Dispatching Four Chinese and Foreign Personnel

To Inspect by Plane Tomorrow

To Implement Relief Measures

Yesterday morning at 8:00 AM, Mr. Song Ziwen convened a meeting of the Yellow River Flood Relief Committee at his residence. Last week, the committee, based on aerial survey maps of the disaster area provided by the General Staff Headquarters, dispatched disaster relief, work relief, and medical relief teams to conduct on-site investigations. Each team has been submitting daily reports to Shanghai. Currently, the committee, based on these reports and reports from various provincial authorities and charitable organizations, has decided on a policy of implementing disaster relief, work relief, and medical relief simultaneously. The disaster relief will focus on providing food, clothing, and sanitation, while the work relief will initially focus on堵塞breaching points. Areas in Jinan and Ningyang in Shandong, and Lanfeng in Henan, and a certain location in Hebei have been selected for establishing offices. Work has already begun on producing 100,000 sets of cotton clothing to protect disaster victims from the cold. The sanitation teams are also organized and ready, and will depart for various areas in a few days. It is reported that the committee has only 4 million yuan allocated by the government for relief funds. This will only allow for selective repairs of existing embankments. The fundamental plan for managing the Yellow River requires substantial funds and time, so it must be postponed. It is planned to submit a proposal to the government in the coming days to establish a unified water conservancy organization to manage the nation's waterways, ensuring that rivers like the Yangtze, Huai, and Han can flow freely without flooding. The committee believes that due to the decline in commerce in recent years and the accumulation of disasters, various sectors in the country are either making repeated donations or unable to donate. Therefore, it has been decided not to solicit donations from the public, request the government to establish special disaster taxes, or forcibly deduct salaries from officials for disaster relief purposes. However, the committee will gratefully accept donations from philanthropists willing to contribute, thanking them on behalf of the disaster victims. Current estimates indicate that 6 million square meters of land are submerged, and 2 million people are homeless. The depth of the disaster is truly deplorable. However, the committee's goal is to have the government bear the full cost of all relief efforts. Although this year's Yellow River flood is not as extensive as the Yangtze, Huai, and Han River floods of 1931, the impact of the disaster is severe. The most severely affected provinces are Shandong, Henan, and Hebei. At the end of last month, the Yellow River Conservancy Commission commissioned the Aerial Survey Office of the General Staff Headquarters to survey the disaster area by air. According to their measurements, the area affected by flooding was approximately 6 million square meters. Based on the average population density, approximately 2 million disaster victims were displaced and homeless. However, the water had already receded significantly by then, so the extent of flooding must have been greater when the Yellow River flood was at its peak. For the sake of relief, the National Government will establish a Yellow River Flood Relief Committee under the Executive Yuan to handle disaster relief, work relief, and medical relief. At that time, Minister Song had just returned from a mission to Europe and America. The government, recognizing Song's successful experience in handling the Yangtze River floods, which was admired both domestically and internationally, specially invited Song to be the chairman of the committee. Song, recognizing the widespread suffering of the disaster victims and the urgent need for relief, accepted the position despite his busy schedule. Before departing for the Lushan Conference, he officially assumed office. He dispatched three teams to the disaster area to investigate the situation and appointed Chinese and foreign committee members and selected experienced assistants. It is reported that after Song returned to Shanghai from the Lushan Conference, he immediately began reviewing reports from all sides and planning the implementation of relief efforts. Every morning at 8:00 AM, he convenes key officials of the committee to discuss these matters. The initial plans have been decided, and Liu Ruiheng, Zhou Xiangxian, Xi Dejiong, and a foreign relief expert (name withheld) have been assigned to fly to Jinan and Kaifeng on the 13th to discuss the implementation of relief measures and inspect the latest flood conditions. The organization of the committee is reportedly being finalized, with the following key officials: Zeng Rongpu as the director of the general office and head of the general affairs group, Qin Fen as the head of the finance group, Xi Dejiong as the head of the disaster relief group, Zhou Xiangxian as the head of the work relief group, and Liu Ruiheng as the head of the sanitation group. It is also reported that Edward and An Xianjin, chief committee members dispatched by the China International Famine Relief Commission, arrived in Shanghai to meet with Song and discuss cooperation in relief efforts. The two arrived in Shanghai last night.

Urgently Repairing Baoshan Seawall Requires Over 500,000 Yuan

The Length of the Damaged Section Reaches 2,780 Zhang

The Provincial Allocation of 60,000 Yuan Is Far from Sufficient, Telegram Sent to Nanjing Requesting Funds

The Baoshan County seawall was damaged in many places due to the hurricane on the 2nd of this month. The Construction Department immediately dispatched technician Zhang Junsheng to Baoshan for an on-site inspection. The total length of the damaged section is 2,780 meters. Even temporary repairs require over 500,000 yuan. The provincial allocation of only 60,000 yuan is far from sufficient. The Seawall Protection Committee convened an emergency meeting and decided to send telegrams to the Executive Yuan and the Ministries of Finance and Interior to request funds. The details are as follows:

Length of Damaged Section

After arriving in Baoshan, Construction Department technician Zhang Junsheng, together with county government technician Bao Hui　, local representatives Dong Weicheng, Wu Zhixiao, and Tao Yunming, jointly inspected the damaged sections in detail. The total length of the damaged section is 2,780 zhang and 8 chi. According to this estimate, using two layers of timber and two layers of stone would require over 500,000 yuan. The length of the damaged section is listed as follows:

Relieving Disaster Victims

In Changxing, Ping An, Shitou, and other five sandbars, 50-60% of the houses were destroyed by the lake on the 2nd of the month. All the embankments were destroyed. 50-60 people died and countless were injured. Upon receiving the report, the county government convened a meeting and decided to use 1,000 yuan from the accumulated grain funds for relief. Two representatives from the county government, two from the First District Office, one from the People's Education Center, one from the Property Office, and one from the County Party Headquarters departed at 6:00 AM the day before yesterday to inspect and provide relief.

Seawall Protection Conference

The Baoshan Seawall Protection Committee convened an emergency meeting the day before yesterday. Wang Zhongqi presided over the meeting. The attendees included Tao Qingfeng, Pan Mengqiao, Shi Tongren, Gu Hongru, Bao Siren, Jin Jushan (represented by Pan Mengqiao), Wu Shiqiao (represented by Xu Jizhong), Yuan Xiluo (represented by Bing Yi), Yin Shuqi, and Peng Weizong. The agenda included: (1) The proposal to expand the organization and intensify the work of the committee was approved in principle. Shi Wenran, Yu Yun, and Tao Yunming were appointed to revise the regulations, which will be submitted to the Standing Committee for approval and then submitted to the county government for discussion at the county administrative meeting. (2) The proposal for opinions on post-disaster measures for embankment construction was approved. Tao Yunming was requested to provide detailed explanations of all phase designs and send them to the relevant authorities for consideration and implementation. (3) The current provincial allocation of 60,000 yuan for the seawall emergency repair project is only sufficient to fill collapsed gaps with mud-filled sacks. After one month, there will be no strong winds or waves, and this money will be wasted. The minimum requirement for emergency relief is to use temporary measures, but the cost would be no less than several million yuan. The provincial allocation is insufficient to meet this challenge. A request will be made to the central government for a special allocation to facilitate the commencement of formal construction. (4) How to request funds from the province and the central government for seawall protection was discussed together with the above. It was resolved to send telegrams to the Executive Yuan and the Ministries of Finance and Interior, and to have representatives of various organizations and Zhang Gongquan meet with Minister Song in person to expedite the allocation of funds. Detailed plans for permanent solutions will be telegraphed later. (5) The proposal to contact relevant counties along the seawall to discuss seawall protection measures was approved. Yuan Shushu, Bao Tigan, Feng Maiying, Shi Wenran, and Ling Zhibin were appointed to make separate contacts.

Telegram to Nanjing Requesting Funds

The Baoshan Seawall Protection Committee sent telegrams to the Executive Yuan and the Ministries of Finance and Interior yesterday, stating: "To President Wang of the Nanjing Executive Yuan, Finance Minister Song, and Interior Minister Huang: The Baoshan County seawall, which is over 5,800 zhang long, has not received provincial budget funds for embankment construction for the past eight or nine years. Last year, the Jiangnan Embankment Post-Disaster Committee raised funds to repair the seawall, costing over 270,000 yuan. During the winter, the seawall was damaged, with over 2,700 zhang destroyed and five or six breaches. The previous project was completed less than a year ago, and all the efforts have been wasted. After repeated appeals from officials and citizens, there is only the hope of 60,000 yuan from the province, which is a drop in the bucket. Even for emergency repair plans, only mud-filled sacks can be used to block the gaps. Compared to the two layers of timber and two layers of stone used last year, after experiencing wind and rain, the funds will be wasted. The 60,000 yuan emergency repair project will inevitably collapse under the current autumn tides. For the present, permanent solutions are out of the question. Even for temporary measures, to ensure that residents can sleep soundly, no less than several million yuan are needed. Otherwise, coastal hurricanes and storms will occur every year. Not only will Baoshan, a weak and small county, inevitably sink, but Shanghai, the national economic center, and the wealthy areas of the former Suzhou, Songjiang, and Taicang prefectures will also be transformed into a swamp. We can only earnestly request the central government to take charge and resolve the situation and quickly allocate large sums of money for relief. We await urgent instructions. Detailed plans for permanent solutions will be gathered from experts and submitted later. Respectfully, the Baoshan Seawall Protection Committee. (11th)"

The Overseas Chinese Relief Association in Mexico Cables a Request for Central Government Relief

=Allocate 5 Million from the American Cotton and Wheat Loan=

=The Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission Should Establish Farms and Factories=

=To Accommodate Distressed Overseas Chinese and Increase Production=

The Overseas Chinese Relief Association in Mexico of this city believes that after Mexico implemented anti-Chinese measures, the money accumulated by the hard work of overseas Chinese in Mexico and the businesses painstakingly managed for decades were all looted by the anti-Chinese party. The overseas Chinese have suddenly lost their jobs, and their livelihoods are precarious. In addition to the more than 4,000 people who were expelled from the country and returned home, there are still tens of thousands of compatriots stranded in Mexico. Efforts should be made to seek fundamental relief. Yesterday, the association specifically cabled the Central Political Conference, requesting that 5 million yuan be allocated from the American cotton and wheat loan to be entrusted to the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission to establish farms or factories to accommodate distressed overseas Chinese and increase production. The original cable is recorded below.

Cable to the Central Political Conference

To the Central Political Conference in Nanjing: The current Mexican anti-Chinese party has no regard for international laws or morality. They have openly implemented the abandonment of our 40,000 overseas Chinese in Mexico, arbitrarily imprisoning, violently beating, and even forcibly expelling them. As a result, the money accumulated by the hard work of a lifetime and the businesses painstakingly managed for decades have been looted and confiscated by these people. The misery is indescribable. Our overseas Chinese entrust their lives to foreign countries, barehanded and unable to resist. They can only be subjected to oppression. At present, it is estimated that over 4,000 people have been forcibly expelled from the country, and there are still tens of thousands stranded in Mexico with no way to escape. Urgent fundamental measures should be taken to provide relief and comfort to the distressed overseas Chinese. The government has an absolute responsibility to protect and support overseas Chinese. Therefore, we respectfully cable and implore you to allocate 55 million yuan from the proceeds of the wheat and cotton loans to establish farms or factories for the purpose of providing relief to distressed overseas Chinese in Mexico, to be entrusted to the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission for handling. This measure is also a legitimate expenditure for construction and production. It is unlike the painful, charitable maintenance referred to in the Lushan Conference. We are grateful and still hope for instructions to comfort the people. Huang Zhulin, Chairman of the Shanghai Overseas Chinese Relief Association in Mexico, and all distressed overseas Chinese respectfully kowtow. (Seal)

Cable to the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission

We are pleased and hope that the government will consider the 40,000 distressed overseas Chinese in Mexico who have been discriminated against and bullied by foreigners and are stranded abroad or have lost their jobs and returned home. We earnestly request that 5 million yuan be allocated from the proceeds of the cotton and wheat loan to be entrusted to your commission to establish large-scale farms or factories to accommodate the distressed overseas Chinese who have lost their jobs due to the anti-Chinese measures in Mexico, to maintain their livelihoods and stabilize their morale. We have always admired your commission as the highest leading agency for managing overseas Chinese affairs. We are confident that you will sympathize with this matter of relieving distressed overseas Chinese. In addition to cabling, we specifically cable and earnestly request that your commission propose to the Central Political Conference to achieve the goal of allocating funds for maintenance, to comfort the distressed overseas Chinese and to stabilize public opinion. We await instructions with utmost respect and distress. Huang Zhulin, Chairman of the Shanghai Overseas Chinese Relief Association in Mexico, and all distressed overseas Chinese respectfully kowtow. (Seal)

Minhang Chamber of Commerce Telegraphs Request to Abolish Cotton Business Tax

Yesterday, Zhang Jingling, acting chairman of the Shanghai County Minhang Chamber of Commerce, telegraphed the Ministry and Provincial authorities, respectfully informing the Nanjing Ministry of Finance, Ministry of Industry, and Jiangsu Provincial Government: The Jiangsu Province is reorganizing the cotton business tax, stipulating a tax rate of ten per thousand, and allowing the Business Tax Bureau to conduct essential inspections, which is similar to a disguised likin (internal transit tax) and borders on disturbing commerce. The meaning of business lies in the necessary conditions of offering goods and selling them. Merchants in Location A invest in purchasing cotton, and must first pay tax to transport it. When it is sold in Location B, they must again pay tax to ship it out. Thus, merchants pay tax when transporting and tax when selling. Tax is levied on both entry and exit, resembling a redundant and burdensome system, more severe than the old likin. Furthermore, most cotton is purchased by factories, and the factories' business tax has already been reported and paid in accordance with regulations. Now, imposing another tax on their purchase of cotton feels particularly harsh and burdensome. In recent years, the rural economy has collapsed and commerce has declined. The main reason for this is the influx of foreign cotton and the stagnation of domestic cotton sales. Both the government and the people are seeking solutions. The decline of agriculture and forestry affects the foundation of the nation, and cotton is crucial to the textile industry, not only affecting the livelihoods of farmers but also the clothing and food of the poor. Therefore, to revitalize the rural economy, the first priority is to protect domestic cotton. How can one bear to impose double heavy taxes? It is reasonable to telegraph and earnestly request an immediate order for abolition, to alleviate the difficulties of Jiangsu merchants and safeguard the people's livelihood. The urgency to await orders is extreme. Respectfully, Zhang Jingling, Acting Chairman of the Shanghai County Minhang Chamber of Commerce, kowtows. True Print.

Lake Society Requests Reduction of Land Surveying Fees

The Zhejiang Provincial Government has ordered the Civil Affairs and Finance Departments to investigate and handle.

Petition

The Shanghai Lake Society submits a document to the Zhejiang Provincial Government stating: Presenting this report based on the situation, humbly requesting that you order the Civil Affairs and Finance Departments to consider reducing land surveying fees to alleviate the people's difficulties. The executive committee member Yu Zhongxian proposed that the collection of land surveying fees in Zhejiang Province at a rate of five jiao per mu is too burdensome, and it should be reviewed and submitted for consideration to reduce it, in order to alleviate the people's difficulties and comply with their wishes. This has been received by the Society. Investigating and surveying land is the most important task during the period of political tutelage. The government has a complete plan for implementing weights and measures, and we dare not disagree with the overall plan. However, considering that the people of Zhejiang Province have suffered from frequent floods in recent years and lack savings, let alone the fact that Western Zhejiang, though once rich, has seen its silk, tea, and bamboo shoots decline due to foreign competition, leading to difficulties for both farmers and merchants, causing sighs and lamentations. Furthermore, the surtaxes under the various county land tax items are nearly equal to the principal amount, coupled with house donations, miscellaneous taxes, and fundraising, leaving no peaceful days. One reason is the decision of the provincial budget, which makes it difficult to reduce taxes rashly. Another reason is the increasing foreign aggression, making it even more difficult to sit by and watch things fall apart. The people of both provinces are struggling under the burden and are already unable to cope. However, observing the situation, although they may not be reduced to cannibalism, their appearance is pale and haggard, their brows furrowed, the sound of looms unheard, and the fields contain starving people. Now, suddenly imposing land surveying fees is no less than adding to the people's suffering. The cunning ones will take the opportunity to increase rents and oppress the honest and weak. How can those who rely on perpetual tenancy be able to stop farming in the morning and switch to other occupations in the evening? They will inevitably end up in ditches and gullies. Therefore, the collection of this fee is objectively taken from the landowners, but indirectly collected from the toiling people. Considering the above points, the proposal made by Committee Member Yu is indeed based on unavoidable circumstances. After discussion at the first regular meeting of the Society's Standing Committee, it was decided to petition your government to consider reducing land surveying fees to alleviate the people's difficulties. This has been recorded. May we humbly request your consideration and order the Civil Affairs and Finance Departments to make a reduction to alleviate the people's difficulties? We hereby submit this document for your review and implementation. Respectfully submitted to Chairman Lu of the Zhejiang Provincial Government, by Chen Qicai, Chairman of the Lake Society Committee.

Reply Telegram

The Zhejiang Provincial Government replies in a telegram stating: To Mr. Chen Aishi of the Shanghai Lake Society Committee: Your letter has been received. Regarding whether land surveying fees can be reduced, we have ordered the Civil Affairs and Finance Departments to jointly investigate and handle the matter. This is a special reply. Lu Dipin, Chairman of the Zhejiang Provincial Government. Secret two seals.

Closing of the Office of the Chief Captain of the Aviation Association Recruitment Team

Since the end of February this year, the Chinese Aviation Association appointed Mayor Wu as the Chief Captain of the Shanghai Recruitment Team and hired Wang Xiaolai and 273 others as captains of the recruitment teams.

In early March, they began recruiting members, collecting donations, and organizing the recruitment team office to handle various fundraising matters. However, regarding the recruitment of members by each team, the original deadline was the end of April. Because the recruitment results at that time were less than half of the originally planned two million yuan, to increase the recruitment results, the deadline was extended by one month, and the actual closing was carried out at the end of May. The total results obtained were 1,394,870 yuan, 9 jiao, 1 fen, and 1 li. This number represents the donations pledged by the captains in each report. The actual cash received, as of now, is only 745,098 yuan, 9 jiao, and 7 fen, 5 li, plus US$22,227. The office must urge each team to pay donations and submit various receipts, and continue to pursue special donations from individuals and organizations, which has delayed the closing. Now, the promised donations from each team have been collected successively. There are still a few outstanding, and most of the receipts have also been submitted. The office, in terms of procedures and responsibilities, must publish the recruitment results of each team in detail in the newspapers, including the number of ordinary members, special members, supporting members, and permanent organizational members, and the amount of donations. In addition, a "General Report of Results" must be compiled and published to the citizens of the city. In addition to reading the recruitment efforts of each team in the daily news, there is also a special book available for reference. Enthusiasm for saving the country through aviation should be even more intense, and donations should continue to flow in.

After Ma and Huang, Lei Dafu Assassinated Again

Lei Currently a Secret Investigator for the Municipal Public Security Bureau, Very Active

Yesterday, he was ambushed by enemies, and died instantly from fatal wounds.

丨Three Assassins Fled, a Stray Bullet Wounded a Boy丨

Since Ma Shaowu (aka Lu Keqin), Director of the Special Affairs Section of the Supervisory Office of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, was tragically assassinated, and less than ten days later, Huang Yonghua (aka Qian Yizhang), who worked with Ma, was murdered for the second time, unexpectedly, within a month, another incident occurred yesterday morning. Lei Dafu (aka Jiang Chen), a secret investigator (commonly known as an informant) of the Investigation Unit of the Special Affairs Section of the Supervisory Office, was shot and killed by three thugs at the intersection of Zhonghua Road and Yingxun Road, outside the Xiaoximen (Small West Gate). These three were outstanding talents in handling special affairs cases for the Municipal Public Security Bureau. Now they have been killed one after another. It is not only unfortunate for the three, but also unfortunate for the Municipal Public Security Bureau. The following is an account of the circumstances of Lei Dafu's shooting yesterday.

[Image: Lei Dafu died after being shot (photographed by Xu Tianzhang)]

Young Man Gasping Like a Cow, Situation Urgent

At around 8:50 a.m. yesterday, Zhu Huanwen, a police officer at post number 22 of the second precinct, second division of the Nanshi Public Security Bureau, was on duty at the intersection of Zhonghua Road and Yingxun Road outside Xiaoximen. Suddenly, a large man wearing a white silk shirt approached the officer and claimed to be a supervisor from the Municipal Public Security Bureau. He said that according to a confidential report, there was a secret meeting of communists in the nearby Jiangyin Street and requested the officer to go with him to arrest them. Upon hearing this, the officer thought the matter was important and planned to report to the station first. Unexpectedly, while he was hesitating, he suddenly saw a young man in a Western suit running towards him, gasping like a cow. Seeing this, Officer Zhu was about to order the young man to stop when three gunshots rang out at the same time.

Three Assassins Fled, Young Man Died

As the gunshots rang out, the young man in the Western suit fell to the ground in response. The three assassins, dressed in white shirts and pants, were about forty or fifty yards away. They turned around and fled. Officer Zhu immediately drew his gun and chased after them, firing as he went. In the confusion, none of the shots hit. In an instant, the assassins had disappeared. The large man who claimed to be a supervisor also fled without a trace. Officer Zhu immediately used the telephone to report to the station. Upon hearing the news, Director Tang immediately led a large number of police officers to surround and search the area. He examined the young man in the Western suit and found him lying on the ground at the entrance of number 16 Yingxun Road, with one bullet each in the back of his head, right temple, and left side. He had already died.

Secret Investigator Lei Dafu Confirmed Without Error

The young man was about twenty years old, with a thin face and a long head, and his hair was combed in Western style. He was wearing a blue French suit, a white silk inner shirt with a turned-down collar, gray flannel pants, gray woolen socks, and black leather shoes. He was still tightly holding a police whistle in his left hand, presumably prepared to sound the alarm in case of an accident. Upon further inspection, a registration paper from the Buminguang Eye Hospital was found on his person, with the name Lei Dafu, age 27, written on it. In addition, there were eight silver dollars, six jiao in small coins, a small diary, and a laundry ticket from the Liyun Laundry Company. Nothing else was found. Director Tang quickly reported to the Supervisory Office, and it was then learned that he was indeed Lei Dafu, a secret investigator from the office.

Stray Bullet Wounds Young Boy, Life in Danger

When the thugs fired their guns, a stray bullet struck Lin Gen, an eleven-year-old child of Fu Jialin, a carpenter from Suzhou who lived upstairs in Jin Shuxing's carpentry shop at number 10 on the same road. The bullet hit the child's left side, and the injury was serious. It is feared that his life is in danger. He has been sent to the hospital for treatment. After the incident, reporters made inquiries in all directions. As a result, it was said that since the cases of Ma and Huang, the authorities had been investigating very strictly, and the deceased Lei Dafu had been particularly active. Yesterday, Lei secretly discovered that the main criminals who assassinated Ma and Huang were to meet somewhere in Jiangyin Street. Therefore, he agreed with a supervisor to go and arrest them in order to establish merit. Unexpectedly, when Lei walked to Jiangyin Street, he had already been recognized by someone. He was followed to Yingxun Road and shot to death.

[Image: Archway at the Entrance of the Great World (photographed by Xu Tianzhang)]

Report from the Organizing Committee

I hope everyone will quickly find a way to rescue. At the same time, everyone should take responsibility, be as generous as Mr. Huang, and hope to get the utmost effect within three days." Chen Lengseng said, "After hearing the speeches of Secretary-General Chu and Section Chief Li, in this time of serious national crisis, we should take responsibility to help the country. The great flood of the Republic of China in the 20th year, and the foreign aggression of September 18th and January 28th in the 21st year, have caused a lot of pain to the country. Unexpectedly, this year we are suffering from the Yellow River disaster again. The country's finances and relief efforts are powerless. We have to hope that the national people will rise up to help the government, do their best to publicize and donate, and get through this difficult time."

Increase Entertainment

There is no additional fundraising in the venues. The income from the ticket sales will all be used for relief funds.

Jingbei Garrison Command Moves to Arrest Feng Laosi

Allowed to Move and Escort After Evidence is Presented

Feng Laosi, a Muslim from Shandong Province, also known as Feng Renshou and Feng Renfu, has been running the Xieji Barber Shop on Edward Road, the Zhonghua Bathhouse in Beigaoshou Lane, and the Fuju Transportation Company for years. His business has been developing well. Recently, someone distributed leaflets outside, stating that Feng was originally a bandit in his hometown. Later, because the government was arresting him tightly, he fled to Shanghai. He successively held public positions such as patrolman and road police, and was dismissed one after another. Then, he opened a door to accept apprentices and colluded with railway teahouses to privately sell red pills, morphine, and drugs. Recently, he specialized in transporting Japanese goods, and his behavior was the same as a traitor. The Huizhong Concession Police Department, based on the statements in the leaflets, sent detectives to arrest Feng Laosi and escort him to the First Special District Local Court, requesting detention for investigation. Feng then hired Lawyer Fan Gang to apply for permission to post bail and be released for interrogation. The case was disclosed in the newspapers. After the case was disclosed in the newspapers, the Songhu Garrison Command learned of it. Feng Laosi had committed a major crime in the past and had been at large for a long time. At first, they did not know where he was hiding, so they could not investigate and arrest him. Now that he has been arrested by the police, he should be transferred to the case for interrogation and punishment. Therefore, they sent staff to the court yesterday morning to apply for a transfer. The police then transferred Feng to the Eighth Criminal Court. After Judge Xue heard the case, the police lawyer Wang Yaotang stated the police investigation. He said that no direct evidence had been obtained. As for the Garrison Command's request for transfer, they should be asked to present considerable evidence. The representative of the Garrison Command stated that due to the rush of time, he could not bring the case. Judge Xue then instructed Feng Laosi to be detained temporarily and await the presentation of evidence by the Garrison Command before further processing.

Bomb at Xu Ruiqing's House

Xu Ruiqing, a native of Wuxi, lives at number 1084 Dongyouheng Road, and runs an iron factory for a living. His factory is also located on the same road. Major Fire at Lujiadu, Pudong

= Eight Thousand Jars of Shaoxing Wine Burned, Loss of Thirty Thousand Gold =

= Kangji Winery Not Insured Against Fire, Suffering a Great Loss =

A fire broke out at the Kangji Winery warehouse, number 14 Gaomuqiaobinnan Lane, Lujiadu, Pudong, at 7:15 p.m. last night. It burned for about two hours, destroying most of the thirty-six thatched houses and eighteen tile houses. The remaining few tile houses were also razed to the ground. The loss was more than thirty thousand gold. The details of the destruction are recorded below.

History of the Winery

The winery has been in operation for several years. Initially, the scale was very small. Later, due to the flourishing business year by year, the site was gradually rented and purchased to expand the warehouse. Currently, there are thirty-six thatched warehouses and eighteen tile warehouses, all of which are filled with Shaoxing wine that has been produced, reaching more than 10,000 jars. The construction form of the warehouse, the thatched houses are divided into three rows, twelve rooms each, located to the east of the tile houses, all facing south. The tile houses are built on the west side, connected to the north and south in a row, facing east. The south of the thatched houses still has vacant land, which is used to store empty jars.

Fire Burns for Two Hours

At 7:15 p.m. yesterday, a fire suddenly broke out in the middle row of thatched warehouses. Because the warehouse materials were made of bamboo and straw, it caught fire immediately. In an instant, it penetrated through the roof, and the flames shot straight into the sky, visible from several miles away. When the nearby police officers of the third precinct, second station reported to the station, Director Yang and Inspectors Sun and Tang led the police to the scene to suppress the fire. They negotiated with Director Sun of the nearby Yingchang Match Factory to open the factory's self-contained water tower and connect a 450-foot-long hose to the fire scene for watering. At the same time, the Dongchang Road Pudong District Fire Brigade also sent a pump car to fight the fire. However, the fire was fierce, and the east wind was very strong, making it difficult to extinguish it for a while. In less than half an hour, the thatched warehouses in the front and rear rows had been affected and destroyed, and the tile warehouses in the west, which were close to the thatched houses, also caught fire continuously. Most of it was burned, and the remaining few were knocked down by manpower to prevent it from spreading. The fire began to weaken at around 8 o'clock, but the firefighters were still afraid that the embers would reignite, so they continued to extinguish the fire. The Yingchang factory irrigated a total of seven or eight thousand gallons of water, but the fire brigade took water from the hamlets, which is difficult to calculate. They rescued until 9:30, and when the fire was completely extinguished, they stopped.

Panic of the Neighbors

After the fire broke out, the garbage pond area to the south of the winery was full of Jiangbei thatched sheds. Most of the Jiangbei residents were having dinner when they suddenly saw the fire. They were all extremely panicked. For a while, they supported the old and carried the young, and fled in droves. All the furniture was mostly moved to the open space near the Yingchang factory in the west. The crying and chaos were very disordered. People from all over who were watching the fire came in droves and were extremely crowded. Fortunately, the police officers of the third district, second station maintained their strength, and Zhang, the district head of the third district, also personally supervised the police to protect the area, so no accident occurred, and the fire never crossed the fence surrounding the winery, so the surrounding houses were not affected, which is a great fortune, otherwise it would be unimaginable.

Loss of Thirty Thousand Gold

In this battle, all the burned and demolished houses of the winery, a total of fifty-four tile and thatched houses, containing 10,000 jars of Shaoxing wine, about 8,000 jars were burned. The average cost per jar is about two yuan and seven jiao, and the loss of the jar price is five jiao per jar, totaling nearly 30,000 gold. The thatched houses of thirty-six rooms and the tile houses of eighteen rooms are worth about 5,000 gold. The total loss of 35,000 gold is a precedent in the winery’s opening. After this disaster, the creation is deeply affected, and it is difficult to recover the old view for a while.

Reason Not Found

After the fire was extinguished, Yang Zhongquan, director of the third precinct and second station, instructed the police to bring Wang Zuting, the relief room of the workshop, to the station to investigate the cause of the fire. According to Wang's confession, he is 38 years old, from Ningbo, and has been serving in the workshop for many years. No one usually lives in the warehouse, so the cause of the fire is still difficult to understand, but there is no fire insurance. After obtaining the confession, the director, because the cause of the fire was unknown, continued to send police officers to the neighbors of the fire scene, residents Shi Jihua from Haimen and Zhu Yushan from Shaoxing, numbers 45 and 46, to testify at the station, all saying that when the fire broke out, they were having dinner, and when they walked out of the door, they saw the flames had come out of the roof. The director had no clues as to what caused the fire, and will continue to summon the foremen and other witnesses of the workshop today for further research. He also ordered that the relief room be temporarily kept in the station and wait for the disposal, and prepared a document on the same night to report to the Intelligence Department of the Main Bureau for review.

Record of the Interrogation of a Large Group of Fake Military Officers

= Chief of Staff, Adjutant, and Head of Communications Department, All Present =

= Police File Charges on Three Counts, Postponing Interrogation for Two Weeks =

Yin Bohong, a Shandong native formerly in the military, had retired and was idle. He conspired with Dong Shujin, an Anhui native residing at 21 Kangti Road in the French Concession, and privately set up the headquarters of the Fifth Route Army of the Eastern Weak North Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army in Room 39 of the Huajie East Apartment at 54 Malang Road in the French Concession. Yin and Dong appointed themselves as commander and deputy commander, respectively, and colluded with five ruffians: Zhou Bingrong from Zhejiang, Cui Qujie from Yangzhou, Teng Ganchen from Anhui, Lü Hanwen from Hangzhou, and Wang Peide, assigning them positions such as chief of staff and adjutant. Additionally, Fang Zhen was appointed as the director of the Shanghai Communications Office, issuing appointment letters indiscriminately and defrauding people of money. Among those deceived were Gong Jizong, a local lacquerer residing at 785 Fahua Town in Western Shanghai, Yue Dingchen, an Anhui native who ran a military band business at 58 Huacheng Road, and Qian Rongfeng, all of whom were swindled into accepting appointments as adjutant and captain, paying sums ranging from 20 to 30 yuan. The scheme was discovered by Pu Xuli (transliteration), the head of the investigation section of the French Concession Police Political Department, on the morning of the 9th. At 9:30 AM, he led Chinese detectives Zhao Zibo, Xu Rufa, Wu Zhonghua, and Li Luochuan to search Room 39 of the Huadong Apartment, arresting Yin Bohong, Dong Shujin, Zhou Bingrong, Cui Jie, and Teng Ganchen on the spot. They confiscated appointment letters in the name of the Fifth Route Army of the Northeast Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army, a list of high-ranking officials, blank appointment letters, receipts for issued appointment letters, military certificates, badges, symbols, and correspondence instructions, training circulars, resumes, military uniforms, hats, armed belts, and other evidence. Furthermore, they located the deceived Gong Jizong and Yue Dingchen. They then proceeded to 22 Baoxing Lane, Caishi Street, where they apprehended adjutant Lü Hanwen and Wang Peide, the director of the adjutant office. They also went to Dong Shujin's residence at 21 Kangti Road and confiscated five wooden chops for appointment letters, letters, and documents. Fang Zhen was at large and had not been apprehended. The detectives brought all the arrested individuals to the police station. After interrogation by the head of the Political Department, Yin Bohong confessed that he was 43 years old, from Shandong, and served as the commander of the Fifth Route Army of the Northeast Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army, whose commander-in-chief was Zhu Fuhai, currently stationed at Xifengkou. Dong Shujin confessed that he was 54 years old, from Anhui, residing at 21 Kangti Road, and served as the deputy commander. Zhou Bingkang confessed that he was 39 years old, from Zhejiang, and served as an adjutant. Cui Jie confessed that he was 38 years old, from Yangzhou, and served as a staff officer. Teng Ganchen confessed that he was 38 years old, from Anhui, and served as a staff officer. Lü Hanwen confessed that he was 43 years old, from Hangzhou, and served as an adjutant. Wang Peide confessed that he was 44 years old, served as the director of the adjutant office, and resided at 550 Beile Road. Gong Jizong confessed that he was 31 years old and a lacquerer. On the 4th of this month, Fang Zhen, claiming to be the director of the Shanghai Communications Office of the Fifth Route Army of the Northeast Volunteer Army, told me that the army was establishing an organization and asked me to contribute money. He then appointed me as an adjutant, sending the badge, symbol, and appointment letter to my home, and swindling me out of 20 yuan. Today, I went to the Huadong Apartment to ask Fang for money, but he had already gone to Nanjing to set up an office. I was arrested when I left. Yue Dingchen confessed that he was [] years old, from Anhui, and ran a military band business. They appointed me as a captain and asked me to buy musical instruments, and I was arrested while negotiating. The chief, based on the confessions, determined that Gong and Yue were not involved and ordered them to be released. Yin and the others were detained for further investigation. It was then discovered that Teng Ganchen, one of the defendants, had been sentenced to six months in prison last year for a political case handled by the Chinese authorities in the Chinese Concession. Not long after his release, he committed another crime. Yesterday, the defendants were escorted to the Second Special District Local Court. At 3 PM, Judge Xiong Huiping took the bench in the First Criminal Court and conducted a preliminary hearing. The police lawyer, Gu Shouxi, presented the case, prosecuting them on three counts under the criminal law: disturbing public order, forging documents and seals, and obtaining property by fraud. He stated that the police still needed to conduct a detailed investigation to apprehend the accomplices, requesting a postponement of the hearing for two weeks. The court reviewed the report, briefly questioned the defendants, and adjourned the hearing to the 15th for further investigation. The defendants were returned to custody pending further instructions.

A Police Officer Seeks Revenge

= Cheng Fuyan Shoots Zhou Zhenting =

= Dispute Arises from Search for Red Pills =

Cheng Fuyan, in his twenties and from Beiping, was a police officer at the Qingyun Road Substation of the Fifth District Police Department. Zhou Zhenting, thirty-four years old, from Shandong, was a police officer at the Fifth District Headquarters. Recently, the Fifth District Headquarters received a report that Cheng was running a red pill den inside Zhou Tongxing's carpentry shop in Hongfu Lane, Qingyun Road. Upon receiving the report, the headquarters immediately dispatched police officers to search the shop, but they returned empty-handed. Cheng believed that someone had interfered, claiming that it was Zhou Zhenting who had done so, and harbored intense resentment. Last night at 9 PM, after the guard shift at the substation had ended, Cheng secretly stole a four-inch live-ammunition handgun from the substation's patrol leader. He went to Zhou's post at the intersection of Xibaoxing Road and Qingyun Road to argue with him. After a brief dispute, Cheng pulled out the handgun from his sleeve and fired one shot at Zhou, hitting him in the neck. Zhou immediately collapsed. Nearby patrol officers, having heard the gunshot, rushed to the scene and restrained the assailant, escorting him to headquarters. The injured officer was immediately sent to Tongren Hospital for treatment. It was reported that the bullet was still lodged in his head and would be surgically removed after examination today. The offending police officer is currently detained in the Fifth District, pending investigation and handling.

Zhang Qu'an and His Mother Reconcile as Before

Zhang Qu'an, the son of the late wealthy Nanzun merchant Zhang Shiming, previously initiated litigation by refusing to acknowledge his biological mother, Zhou Miaoying. In the initial two trials, Qu'an was victorious. However, in the third trial, the Supreme Court overturned all previous judgments, stating that a son cannot sever ties with his mother. Zhou Miaoying, having achieved ultimate victory and obtaining legal recognition, initiated a criminal lawsuit against Zhang Xu, the senior wife, accusing her of instigating Qu'an to abandon her. Judge Liu Yugui of the First Special District Local Court held two hearings, summoning Qu'an to testify. However, Qu'an stated that the previous litigation was entirely his own doing and that he deeply regretted it, expressing his willingness to seek mediation through relatives and friends. Consequently, the case was postponed. It has been learned that Zhou and her son recently met at a large hotel in Western Shanghai. Qu'an agreed to fully repay all debts incurred by his biological mother, Zhou Miaoying, over the years, totaling 50,000 yuan. Additionally, he would provide a monthly allowance of 400 yuan for her expenses, rent a house for her to live in, and visit her frequently. From then on, mother and son reconciled as before. Zhou Miaoying instructed her representing lawyer, Yuan Yang'an, to file a motion to withdraw the lawsuit.

Unnamed Man Jumps into the River

Unknown Grievances Lead to this Final Path

The Riqing Company's small steamboat, Anshan No. 9, was sailing back to the Pudong pier from the Guangdong Road wharf at 6 PM the night before. As it was sailing past the French warship moored outside the French Concession, a young man suddenly jumped into the raging waves from the stern without anyone noticing. When the sailors discovered this and reported it, the captain stopped the boat and turned back to rescue him, but the man's body had already sunk and disappeared. The captain, Wang Liansheng, then sailed the boat to the Maritime Customs Water Police Station to report the incident. His name and age are currently difficult to determine.

Worker Crushed to Death by Car

Yesterday afternoon at approximately 12:40 PM, a public bus on Jiading Road in the Hongkou district was passing by when a man dressed in a white cloth shirt and trousers, about twenty-two or twenty-three years old and resembling a worker, was riding a bicycle towards the bus. He was unable to avoid it in time and was knocked to the ground by the bus, suffering a severe head injury that resulted in immediate death. Bidding for New Furniture for the Municipal Government Opens

Shuimingchang Wins the Bid

The Shanghai Municipal Government is scheduled to hold a completion ceremony for its new building on Double Ten Day and move to the central urban area on New Year's Day. The existing furniture is insufficient, and the government advertised for contractors to handle the procurement. Extension of Tap Water Pipes in Jiangwan

Public Works and Health Bureaus Draft Plans

The Shanghai Municipal Public Works Bureau has repeatedly received petitions from various organizations in Jiangwan requesting that the Zhabei Power Plant extend the town's tap water pipes. However, the company requires a subsidy of 4,000 yuan, which has caused the project to be delayed for a long time. As the Health Committee is about to be established, the water pipe issue urgently needs to be addressed. The Public Works Bureau and Health Bureau convened a meeting with all relevant parties to discuss solutions. Those who attended included Wu Mengqin and Gu Shanzhang from the Jiangwan District Municipal Committee, local gentry Cai Xiangsun and Li Shoupeng from Jiangwan, and Weng Yousan from the Water and Electricity Company. After discussion, the company stated that a subsidy of 4,000 yuan was still required. However, the Jiangwan area has suffered from commercial depression and economic hardship since the war, making fundraising extremely difficult. They strongly requested a reduction in the subsidy. Subsequently, the Public Works Bureau and Health Bureau proposed a compromise solution: the bureaus would request the Municipal Government to allocate 1,000 yuan as a subsidy, and the remaining amount would be raised locally within three months. If this proves impossible, the Municipal Government's subsidy would be used to prepare water transport vehicles and hire workers for transportation so that citizens in the area can purchase water.

Navigation Information After the Opening of the Pu Zhao River Dam

Tongli Shipping Bureau Opens Shipping Routes Between Xu and Si

The Pu Zhao and Pu Hui Rivers in Western Shanghai, the eastern and western thoroughfares of the former Song County, had been silted up for years due to lack of dredging. Ma Xiangbo and Zhang Weichen requested the National Government's Shanghai Post-War Rehabilitation Council to allocate funds for dredging. The dam was opened at the beginning of the month, and after the rivers were connected, travel and shipping gradually became more frequent. Merchant Ma Youde has raised funds to organize the Tongli Shipping Bureau, launching steamships between Xujiahui and Sijing, connecting to steamships to Qingpu, Zhujiajiao, Songjiang, and Chenshan via Hongqiao and Qibao. The inaugural voyage took place the day before yesterday. The ship is named "De Da" and has an engine power of fourteen horsepower, with a speed of thirty li per hour. Currently, there is one round trip between Xujiahui and Sijing each day. The ship departs from Xujiahui at 7 AM, arriving at 10 AM, and departs from Sijing at 1 PM, arriving at 3 PM. The Xujiahui wharf is located at the pier of the Catholic Church. Currently, the ship is undergoing trial voyages, and it is planned to increase the number of trips in the future. The fares are very low, with the entire journey costing only four dimes. Passengers traveling from Shanghai to the western, northern, and southern countryside are very crowded, and the cargo volume is also large. All sectors praise the convenience.

Record of the Shareholders' Meeting of the China Commerce & Credit Trust Co.

The China Commerce & Credit Trust Co. held its third annual shareholders' meeting on September 10th. The meeting place was located upstairs at 521 Yuxing Lane, Nanjing Road, where the company is housed. Shareholders attending included Shen Xintian, Dai Xidi, Zhang Ruisheng, He Zhenyuan, Tu Hongjun, Wang Qinji, Luo Renji, Yao Chengji, and several others, totaling dozens of people. The meeting convened at 3 PM. The number of attendees and their shares exceeded a majority. Shen Xintian was publicly elected as chairman. (1) The supervisor reported on the accounts, and the balance sheet and certificate from Accountant Wang Haifan were distributed to each shareholder, with no objections raised. (2) General Manager Gu reported that since the company's establishment, business has been difficult due to the current situation, and that the second installment of shares has not yet been fully collected. After repeated discussions by the shareholders, it was resolved to reduce the company's capital to 250,000 yuan, assess the current assets at their actual value, and hand them over to the new board of directors for processing. The shortfall would be the responsibility of General Manager Gu, who would raise new shares and register with the ministry. (3) General Manager Gu stated his difficulties and resigned from his position. After deliberation, the shareholders urged him to persevere, and a unanimous show of hands approved. (4) A shareholder proposed that several shareholders recently requested a transfer of ownership. After discussion, it was resolved that, in accordance with company law, a transfer of ownership could not be made until formal shares were issued. (5) The election of directors and supervisors. It was provisionally resolved to maintain the current status of the original directors and supervisors until new shares were added, and then re-elect them. After the above resolutions were passed, the meeting adjourned, by which time it was already 6 o'clock.

Kidnappers Request Withdrawal of Appeal

Fearing Possible Failure Leading to a Death Sentence

Wang Yuanwei, a Shaoxing native and kidnapper, colluded with accomplices to kidnap Wang Gaosun's nine-year-old beloved son, Wang Delin, from 2 Dafeng Lane, Huanlong Road, French Concession, on December 28th of last year. The case was cracked by the British Concession Police. Wang was also involved in a kidnapping case in the British Concession and was sent to the First Special Court, where he was sentenced to life imprisonment. Subsequently, the police transferred him to the Second Special Court, where he was found guilty and sentenced to 21 years in prison. Wang refused to accept the verdict and filed an appeal with the Third Branch of the High Court. The High Court, based on the report, held an investigation hearing at 2 PM yesterday, with Judge Fan Peien presiding. Wang and accomplices Sun Xiaomao and Yao Sheng, who had already been convicted and were being executed, were brought in, along with witnesses including Wang Chen, the victim's mother, the young victim Wang Delin, and the detectives from the police station who handled the case. During the hearing, Wang suddenly stated in court that he was withdrawing the appeal and requested that the sentences imposed in the British Concession be combined and served in the French Concession prison. The court approved the withdrawal of the appeal and ordered a ruling on the consolidated execution. After the hearing, reporters asked Wang why he had suddenly withdrawn the appeal. He replied that he knew that his crime was real and that he was lucky to be sentenced to prison. If the appeal failed and he was sentenced to death, it would be even more unjust. Therefore, he was willing to withdraw the appeal and serve his sentence peacefully in prison, hoping to be pardoned when a general amnesty occurred. After he finished speaking, he was taken back to the detention center by the police to await the ruling.

Inspection Report of Two Banks

The Central Bank's 172nd Report on Issuance Reserves states: "In accordance with Article 15 of the Central Bank Ordinance, this council is responsible for inspecting the reserve funds for the exchange coupons issued by this bank. Today, September 9, 1933, the 172nd inspection was held at the Issuance Bureau of this bank, and the results of the inspection are hereby announced as follows: (A) The total amount of exchange coupons issued is 56,800,258.1 yuan, including silver yuan coupons of 51,900,651.1 yuan and subsidiary currency coupons of 4,896,070 yuan. The total amount of exchange coupon reserves is 56,800,258.1 yuan, including cash reserves of 46,588,581 yuan. The cash reserves include 42,196,959 yuan stored in the issuance vault of this bank, 2,588,131 yuan stored in branches of this bank in various ports, and 1,800,349.1 yuan stored in fellow banks. The guarantee reserves are equivalent to 10,214,000 yuan in silver yuan. (B) The total amount of customs gold exchange coupons issued is 417,269.4 yuan. The total amount of customs gold exchange coupon reserves is 417,269.4 yuan, including 7,004.69 taels of standard gold valued at 59,570,000, resulting in customs gold of 417,269.4 yuan. According to Article 2 of the Central Bank Exchange Coupon Regulations, 60% of the reserve should be in cash and 40% should be in guarantees. The results of this inspection show that the cash reserve exceeds 60% and the guarantee reserve is less than 40%, which is in accordance with the regulations. This report is hereby issued. September 9, 1933, Li Fusun, Chairman of the Board of Supervisors of the Central Bank; Xie Mingxun, Supervisor; Bei Songsun, Supervisor; Qin Runqing, Supervisor; Yu Zhiqing, Supervisor; Lin Kanghou, Supervisor; Xu Jiyu, Supervisor."

The China Industrial Bank's 25th Report on Issuance Reserves states: "The China Industrial Bank's issuance department reserves have always been completely separate from the business department's funds, and the reserves are fully sufficient. The issuance reserve figures for September 9, 1933, are hereby announced as follows: The total amount of exchange coupons issued is 28,953,761 yuan, including 15,657,761 yuan issued by this bank, 5,956,000 yuan issued by affiliated banks, and 7,340,000 yuan claimed by various banks and firms. Except for the portion claimed by various banks and firms, which is inspected according to the original method, this inspection covers the issuance amount of exchange coupons issued by this affiliated bank, totaling 21,613,761 yuan. The reserve amount for exchange coupons issued by this affiliated bank totals 21,613,761 yuan, including cash reserves of 13,200,3961 yuan and guarantee reserves of 8,400,980 yuan. The cash reserve accounts for more than 60%, and the guarantee reserve accounts for less than 40%, both of which have been checked and found to be correct. Inspector Zhang Yiyan, accountant at the Zhengze Accounting Firm."

The silk and satin department has newly released electric-printed silk crepe cheongsam material, priced at $2 per piece. Other goods in the knitting and cotton departments are also sold at flat prices, so the store has been crowded with customers every day, barely able to keep up.

Publishing Industry

The First Issue of the Shanghai Gazetteer Quarterly is About to be Published: Shanghai's position in the international community is becoming increasingly important. The Shanghai Gazetteer Office, which conducts detailed research on Shanghai, has an increasingly important mission. After the office published the first issue of the Shanghai Gazetteer Quarterly in June this year, the entire country recognized the office's mission and the nature of its work. It is now learned that the office's second issue will be published in mid-September. The length of the issue has increased by 50% compared to the first issue, and the content is extremely rich: (1) "Shanghai's Rainfall" uses detailed statistics from the past 60 years and records from ancient books as a basis for research; (2) "The Shanghai British and American Concessions in the Taiping Heavenly Kingdom Era" details the state of the Public Concession before its formation; (3) "The Growing Period of the Shanghai French Concession" records the gradual growth of the French Concession after its establishment, including the first Ningbo Guild Hall bloodbath, which is extremely important; (4) "The Disturbance in the Public Court" is similar to the May 30th Massacre and is an important historical event in the anti-imperialist movement of the Shanghai people; (5) "Shanghai's Domestic Banks" is a very accurate investigation from the establishment of domestic banks in Shanghai to the present; (6) "Outline of Shanghai Arts and Crafts"; (7) "Shanghai's Periodicals"; both of these are continuations of the first issue; (8) "Compilation Outline of Local Customs" is an appendix. National gazetteer offices, university libraries, and registered academic institutions that need this quarterly can request it from the Shanghai Gazetteer Office at 291 Sapobao Road, Shanghai. It is best to include registered postage to avoid loss.

New Century Bookstore Releases Five New Books: The New Century Bookstore at the intersection of Nanjing Road and Yunnan Road in Deyu Lane was founded by Zhang Xinying. Since its opening, the bookstore's business has been thriving. It sells no fewer than 200 kinds of new and old novels, all at particularly low prices, and also offers various exquisite gifts. Recently, it has released five major new books: Newly Edited Northeast Hero, Oriental Divine Hero, Dew Relationship, Overseas Fairyland Record, and Mr. Zhang Xianshui's famous novel New Analysis of Tiger Biography. Each set has four large volumes and sells for only one dollar and ten cents. Mail orders from other locations are accepted.

Medical and Pharmaceutical Fields

Zhu Nanshan's Medical Office Relocates: Chinese medicine doctor Zhu Nanshan recently built a new house across from Xu Chongdao Pharmacy on Avenue Édouard VII and relocated there a few days ago. Also, the wife of Yin Zhanqing, a detective from the Wayside Police Station, suffered from severe metrorrhagia this summer. Repeated attempts by famous Chinese and Western doctors to save her were ineffective. Later, Zhu Nanshan and his son were invited to jointly diagnose and treat her, and she recovered suddenly. Yesterday, she specially presented a plaque with the inscription "Wonderful Hands Bring Back Spring," and the military band played loudly, making it quite lively.

Guo Taihua Hospital Resumes Regular Clinic Hours: Guo Taihua Gynecology Hospital, founded by the famous female gynecologist Guo Taihua, had previously shortened its daily clinic hours due to the hot summer. Now that the weather has turned cool in autumn, for the convenience of patients, it has resumed regular clinic hours from the day before yesterday: 10:00 AM to 12:00 PM and 2:00 PM to 6:00 PM daily, and 2:00 PM to 4:00 PM on Sunday afternoons. Hospitalization for treatment and childbirth is available at any time.

Calligraphy and Painting News

Third Session of Lü Gongwang's Calligraphy Correspondence Course Deadline: Lü Gongwang of Beiping, since he established the foundation of holding a pen for learning, has been running a correspondence course, seeking simplicity, efficiency, and speed. Each method and technique uses a scientific approach, teaching according to individual qualities and characteristics. All those who follow it and work hard for several hundred hours can usually develop a kind of formal script. Specialized students can grasp the essence of any tablet inscription, truly breaking through the ancient and modern difficulties of writing. Students from the previous two sessions have been all over the country and abroad, and their achievements have all been announced publicly. This session is also coming to a close. However, it is heard that Mr. Lü is old and may not be able to continue running the course.

Letter

To the Honorable Editor: I recently read a flyer published in the Shen Bao on September 10th, stating that Feng Laosi was a traitor and had been arrested by the police, involving the Fuji Transportation Company, etc. The words were extremely shocking. It has been verified that the Fuji Transportation Company in Gaoshou Lane was organized by Du Youliang and Chen Jinrong in 1927. It joined the trade association as a member and submitted a request to the Social Bureau to transfer it to the Municipal Government for registration, and it obtained a license as proof. The items transported by our company are exclusively engaged in the fruit business on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway. Other rival loans and contraband goods are not transported. This can be investigated. Moreover, our company has never known Feng Laosi. How can we be involved out of thin air? Except for other parts of Feng Laosi, we will not hear about it. All of Feng Laosi's opening of the Fuji Transportation Company does not match the facts and damages our company's reputation. I hereby submit a letter to clarify the situation and ask the Honorable Editor to correct the situation to reveal the truth. Respectfully yours, Du Youliang and Chen Jinyuan of the Fuji Transportation Company, September 11th.

Examination Committee for Land and Water Maps of the Ministry of Education

The Ministry of Education and the Ministry of Interior jointly formed an Examination Committee for Land and Water Maps. The Ministry of Education appointed Li Yiyan and Zheng Dasheng as expert examination members.

Jiaotong University Establishes a Research Branch in Peiping

(Nanjing Dispatch, 11th) Jiaotong University established a research institute at its main campus in Shanghai in 1928. The university has now also established a research branch at Jiaotong University's Peiping Institute, temporarily setting up an Economic Research Department, which will be staffed by the institute's professors. The budget is set at 700 yuan per month and was officially established on September 1st, reported to the Ministry of Railways for record. In addition, the museum instruments and models of the university's Peiping Institute have now been transported to Peiping in full due to the stability of North China.

A Grand Review Will Be Held on April 4th Next Year

Chinese Workers in the Soviet Union Receive Education

(TASS, Vladivostok, September 10) A special school has been established in Irkutsk to train teachers to use Romanized Chinese letters. The first group of teachers has already graduated. The school's work is to enable educational institutions in the Far East to accelerate their work of eliminating illiteracy among Chinese workers in the Soviet Far East. As of August 1 this year, 30 ordinary literacy classes using Romanized Chinese letters have been established in Vladivostok, with a duration of three months. 1,500 Chinese have been taught to read and write. Graduates of ordinary literacy classes can enter specialized schools to receive general education. There are currently three such specialized schools in Vladivostok.

The Committee for Romanized Chinese Letters has published a primary dictionary of Romanized culture and a Chinese-Russian dictionary, as well as several other school textbooks using Roman letters.

This City

The Municipal Education Bureau Distributes Application Forms for Subsidies to Private Schools

Deadline is September 16th

The Municipal Education Bureau has always had a rule to forward requests to the municipal government for discretionary subsidies to private primary and secondary schools in the city that are well-managed, duly registered, and in need of subsidies. Now that the 22nd year is about to begin, the bureau has long stipulated the form for the subsidy and ordered the schools to fill it out on time so that it can be reviewed and handled. The forms have begun to be distributed from yesterday, and the deadline is September 16th, which is not far away. Therefore, schools that need to apply for the subsidy should go to the bureau to collect the forms and submit them to the bureau for review before the end of this month. However, schools that have been approved by the Public Concession and have been granted subsidies will no longer be granted the subsidy by the bureau due to limited funding.

The Public Concession Will Increase Education Subsidies

Regarding the issue of the Public Concession Bureau subsidizing private primary and secondary schools within its borders, according to the Central News Agency reporter, according to Lin Kanghou of the Chinese Committee, the bureau allocates 150,000 taels of silver each year, with approximately 100,000 yuan going to Chinese schools, followed by Japanese schools. Recently, the bureau intends to increase the appropriation in response to requests from all sectors. It will be submitted for discussion at the Education Committee meeting at 3:00 PM this Wednesday. As for the Girls' Middle School on Medhurst Road, it plans to expand and has purchased more than ten acres of land on Harbin Road to build school buildings. The construction cost is set at 200,000 yuan and has been formally approved. Construction will begin in the near future. It is also learned that the Public Concession will establish a Chinese school in the near future.

The Location Will Be in the City Center

In order to assess the achievements of Boy Scouts throughout the city over the past year and seek future improvements, the Municipal Boy Scout Council convened an emergency meeting the day before yesterday to discuss measures. Shanghai Branch of the Educational Film Association

Showing Educational Films is About to Become a Reality

Starting October 1st, three machines will depart to show films in 15 schools each day

Public Education Film Association and Children's Education Film Hall are currently under preparation

The Shanghai Branch of the Chinese Educational Film Association has scheduled to start showing educational films in schools by rotation starting on October 1. The details have already been published in various newspapers. It is learned that the association is actively preparing because of the urgency of the period. At the same time, it is also preparing to hold public education film festivals and children's education film halls. The preparation situation is recorded as follows.

Touring Schools for Screenings: The association has decided to start touring schools in this city to show educational films on a rotational basis from October 1. Three projectors will depart each day to show films in five schools each, 15 schools a day. All schools in the city can be screened within 12 days. Each school will be rotated once every two weeks. The fee is one yuan per semester for university students, five cents for middle school students, and five cents per session for elementary school students. All films have been borrowed from foreign countries and are currently being carefully selected. The screening venues are in the large auditoriums of the schools. If there are no large auditoriums, then nearby public places will be used.

Children's Education Film Hall: The Children's Education Film Hall will also begin operating in mid-October. The city will be divided into five districts: east, south, west, north, and center. One location will be established in each district. Temporarily, appropriate cinemas will be borrowed as screening venues. Two screenings will be held simultaneously in each district every Sunday morning. The fee is five cents per person.

Public Education Film Festival: In order to give ordinary citizens the opportunity to watch educational films and to supplement the shortcomings of social education, the association is also preparing to hold public education film festivals, which will also be held in five districts: east, south, west, north, and center. The screening locations will be public places such as public education halls and lakesides. It will be held once a week. Before the start, a large-scale public education film publicity conference will be held to arouse public attention, and leaders from all walks of life will be invited to visit and speak.

The Senior Vocational School at the Former Labor University Site Officially Opened Yesterday

A portion of the Jiangwan campus property of the former National Labor University has been officially allocated by the central government to National Tongji University, with instructions to establish a senior vocational school affiliated with the university. The school has been officially established and university professors have been appointed to concurrently serve as directors. It is divided into two departments: mechanical engineering and civil engineering, and admits junior high school graduates. A hundred students have been admitted through examinations and classes officially began yesterday (September 11th). Most of the teachers are concurrently professors at Tongji University, many of whom studied in Germany and possess high academic qualifications. The curriculum is also quite comprehensive. The school originally had five factories: an iron factory, a printing factory, a rubber factory, a can factory, and a mast lamp factory. The iron factory is the largest in scale and can be called the leader of vocational schools. In the future, the graduates will surely be welcomed by society.
